PR Writing in Python
  • 🧑

    Human

    Extend BeeAI - Framework by adding a built-in deployment module that allows any BeeAI agent to be served as a production-ready API without manually writing FastAPI wrappers. Implement a simple interface such as agent.serve() or serve_agent(agent) that automatically exposes /run, /stream, /health, and /metrics endpoints with proper JSON responses and error handling. Additionally, add a CLI command (e.g., beeai deploy init) that generates a minimal but production-ready Dockerfile and docker-compose configuration for containerized deployment. Keep the implementation modular and fully backward-compatible, ensuring that existing agent functionality remains unchanged while making it significantly easier to deploy BeeAI agents as microservices.
    beeai-framework/

beeai_framework.utils import AbortSignal 16 from beeai_framework.utils.dicts import exclude_keys 17 18 19 class RunnableOptions(TypedDict, total=False): 20 """Options for a runnable.""" 21 22 signal: AbortSignal 23 """The runnable's abort signal data.""" 24 25 context: dict[str, Any] 26 """Context can be used to pass additional context to runnable.""" 27 28 29 class RunnableOutput(BaseModel): 30 """Runnable output.""" 31 32 model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow") 33 34 output: list[InstanceOf[AnyMessage]] 35 """The runnable output.""" 36 37 context: dict[str, Any] = {} 38 """Context can be used to return additional data by runnable.""" 39 40 @property 41 def last_message(self) -> AnyMessage: 42 """Returns the latest message in output, with a fallback if it is not defined.""" 43 44 last_message = self.output[-1] if self.output else None 45 return last_message or AssistantMessage("") 46 47 48 R = TypeVar("R", bound=RunnableOutput) 49 P = ParamSpec("P") 50 51 52 class Runnable(Generic[R], ABC): 53 """A unit of work that can be invoked using a stable interface. 54 55 Attributes: 56 _middlewares: The list of middleware to be used when executing the runnable. 57 """ dictionary that can be used to pass additional context to the runnable 71 72 Returns: 73 The runnable output. 74 """ 75 pass 76 77 @property 78 @abstractmethod 79 def emitter(self) -> Emitter: 80 """The event emitter for the runnable.""" 81 pass 82 83 @property 84 def middlewares(self) -> list[RunMiddlewareType]: 85 """The list of middleware to be used when executing the runnable.""" 86 return self._middlewares 87 88 89 def runnable_entry(handler: Callable[P, Awaitable[R]]) -> Callable[P, Run[R]]: 90 """A decorator that wraps the runnable into an execution context. 91 92 For example: 93 94 @runnable_entry 95 async def run(self, input: list[AnyMessage], /, **kwargs: Unpack[RunnableOptions]) -> RunnableOutput: 96 ctx = RunContext.get() 97 # ... runnable logic ... 98 return RunnableOutput(output=...) 99 """ 100 101 @functools.wraps(handler) 102 def wrapper(*args: P.args, **kwargs: P.kwargs) -> Run[R]: 103 """Wrapper that automates the call to RunContext.enter().""" 104 105 async def inner(ctx: RunContext) -> R: 106 # Use potentially modified input from run_params instead of original args 107 modified_input = ctx.run_params.get("input", args[1] if len(args) > 1 else None) 108 modified_args = (args[0], modified_input, *args[2:]) 109 # pyrefly: ignore [invalid-param-spec] 110 return await handler(*modified_args, **kwargs) 111 112 self = args[0] if args else None 113 if not isinstance(self, Runnable): 114 raise TypeError("The first argument of a runnable's run method must be a Runnable instance.") 115 116 if len(args) < 2: 117 raise ValueError("The positional input argument is required.") 118 119 runnable_kwargs: RunnableOptions = kwargs # type: ignore 120 return ( 121 RunContext.enter( 122 self, 123 inner, 124 signal=runnable_kwargs.get("signal", None), 125 run_params={"input": args[1], **exclude_keys(kwargs, {"signal", "input"})}, 126 ) 127 .middleware(*self.middlewares) 128 .context(runnable_kwargs.get("context") or {}) 129 ) 130 131 return wrapper Only set _predecessor if cause is a FrameworkError 55 self._predecessor = cause if isinstance(cause, FrameworkError) else None 56 self.__cause__ = cause 57 self.context = context or {} 58 59 @property 60 def predecessor(self) -> BaseException | None: 61 return self._predecessor or self.__cause__ 62 63 @staticmethod 64 def is_retryable(error: Exception) -> bool: 65 """is error retryable?.""" 66 if isinstance(error, FrameworkError): 67 return error.retryable 68 return not isinstance(error, CancelledError) 69 70 @staticmethod 71 def is_fatal(error: BaseException) -> bool: 72 """is error fatal?""" 73 if isinstance(error, FrameworkError): 74 return error.fatal 75 else: 76 return False 77 78 def name(self) -> str: 79 """get name (class) of this error""" 80 return type(self).__name__ 81 82 def has_fatal_error(self) -> bool: 83 current_exception: BaseException | None = self 84 85 while current_exception is not None: 86 if FrameworkError.is_fatal(current_exception): 87 return True 88 89 current_exception = current_exception.__cause__ 90 91 return False 92 93 def traverse(self) -> Generator["FrameworkError", None, None]: 94 next: FrameworkError | BaseException | None = self # Use | for union 95 while isinstance(next, FrameworkError): 96 yield next 97 next = next.predecessor 98 99 def get_cause(self) -> BaseException: 100 deepest_cause: BaseException = self 101 102 while deepest_cause.__cause__ is not None: 103 deepest_cause = deepest_cause.__cause__ 104 105 return deepest_cause 106 107 def explain(self) -> str: 108 output = [] 109 110 for offset, error in enumerate(self.traverse()): 111 message = _format_error_message(error, offset=offset) 112 output.append(message) 113 114 if error and error.predecessor: 115 message = _format_error_message(error.predecessor, offset=offset + 1, strip_traceback=False) 116 output.append(message) 117 118 return "\n".join(output).strip() 119 120 @classmethod 121 def ensure( 122 cls, error: Exception, *, message: str | None = None, context: dict[str, Any] | None = None 123 ) -> "FrameworkError": 124 if isinstance(error, FrameworkError): 125 error.context.update(context or {}) 126 return error 127 128 if isinstance(error, CancelledError): 129 return AbortError(cause=error, context=context) 130 131 if message: 132 return cls(cause=error, message=message, context=context) 133 else: 134 return cls(cause=error, context=context) 135 136 async def clone(self) -> Self: 137 cloned = type(self)( 138 self.message, 139 is_fatal=self.fatal, 140 is_retryable=self.retryable, 141 cause=await self.__cause__.clone() if isinstance(self.__cause__, FrameworkError) else self.__cause__, 142 context=self.context.copy(), 143 ) 144 return cloned 145 146 147 class AbortError(FrameworkError, CancelledError): 148 """Raised when an operation has been aborted.""" 149 150 def __init__( 151 self, 152 message: str = "Operation has been aborted!", 153 *, 154 cause: BaseException | None = None, 155 context: dict[str, Any] | None = None, 156 ) -> None: 157 super().__init__(message, is_fatal=True, is_retryable=False, cause=cause, context=context) 158 159 160 __all__ = ["AbortError", "FrameworkError"] 161

1 # Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC 2 # SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 3 4 import logging 5 import sys 6 from logging import Formatter 7 from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any 8 9 from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError 10 from beeai_framework.utils.config import CONFIG 11 12 13 class LoggerError(FrameworkError): 14 """Raised for errors caused by logging.""" 15 16 def __init__( 17 self, 18 message: str = "Logger error", 19 *, 20 cause: Exception | None = None, 21 context: dict[str, Any] | None = None, 22 ) -> None: 23 super().__init__(message, is_fatal=True, is_retryable=False, cause=cause, context=context) 24 25 26 class LoggerFormatter(Formatter): 27 def format(self, record: logging.LogRecord) -> str: 28 if hasattr(record, "is_event_message") and record.is_event_message: 29 return logging.Formatter( 30 "{asctime} | {levelname:<8s} |{message}", 31 style="{", 32 datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S", 33 ).format(record) 34 else: 35 return logging.Formatter( 36 "{asctime} | {levelname:<8s} | {name}:{funcName}:{lineno} - {message}", 37 style="{", 38 datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S", 39 ).format(record) 40 41 42 class Logger(logging.Logger): 43 if TYPE_CHECKING: 44 trace = logging.Logger.debug 45 46 def __init__(self, name: str, level: int | str = CONFIG.log_level) -> None: 47 self.add_logging_level("TRACE", logging.DEBUG - 5) 48 49 super().__init__(name, level) 50 51 console_handler = logging.StreamHandler(stream=sys.stdout) 52 console_handler.setFormatter(LoggerFormatter()) 53 54 self.addHandler(console_handler) 55 56 # https://stackoverflow.com/questions/2183233/how-to-add-a-custom-loglevel-to-pythons-logging-facility/35804945#35804945 57 def add_logging_level(self, level_name: str, level_num: int, method_name: str | None = None) -> None: 58 """ 59 Comprehensively adds a new logging level to the `logging` module and the 60 currently configured logging class. 61 62 `level_name` becomes an attribute of the `logging` module with the value 63 `level_num`. `method_name` becomes a convenience method for both `logging` 64 itself and the class returned by `logging.getLoggerClass()` (usually just 65 `logging.Logger`). If `method_name` is not specified, `level_name.lower()` is 66 used. 67 68 To avoid accidental clobberings of existing attributes, this method will 69 return without action if the level name is already an attribute of the 70 `logging` module or if the method name is already present 71 72 Example 73 ------- 74 >>> add_logging_level('TRACE', logging.DEBUG - 5) 75 >>> logging.getLogger(__name__).setLevel("TRACE") 76 >>> logging.getLogger(__name__).trace('that worked') 77 >>> logging.trace('so did this') 78 >>> logging.TRACE 79 5 80 81 """ 82 if not method_name: 83 method_name = level_name.lower() 84 85 if hasattr(logging, level_name): 86 # already defined in logging module 87 return 88 if hasattr(logging, method_name): 89 # already defined in logging module 90 return 91 if hasattr(logging.getLoggerClass(), method_name): # pragma: no cover 92 # already defined in logger class 93 return 94 95 # This method was inspired by the answers to Stack Overflow post 96 # http://stackoverflow.com/q/2183233/2988730, especially 97 # http://stackoverflow.com/a/13638084/2988730 98 def log_for_level(self: logging.Logger, message: str, *args: int, **kwargs: Any) -> None: # pragma: no cover 99 if self.isEnabledFor(level_num): 100 self._log(level_num, message, args, stacklevel=2, **kwargs) 101 102 def log_to_root(message: str, *args: int, **kwargs: Any) -> None: # pragma: no cover 103 logging.log(level_num, message, *args, **kwargs) 104 105 logging.addLevelName(level_num, level_name) 106 setattr(logging, level_name, level_num) 107 setattr(logging.getLoggerClass(), method_name, log_for_level) 108 setattr(logging, method_name, log_to_root) 109 110 111 __all__ = ["Logger", "LoggerError"] 112

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

from typing import Any

from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError


class DeploymentError(FrameworkError):
    """Base error for deployment-related issues."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str = "Deployment error",
        *,
        cause: BaseException | None = None,
        context: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        super().__init__(message, is_fatal=False, is_retryable=True, cause=cause, context=context)


class AgentExecutionError(DeploymentError):
    """Raised when agent execution fails."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str = "Agent execution failed",
        *,
        cause: BaseException | None = None,
        context: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        super().__init__(message, cause=cause, context=context)


class ValidationError(DeploymentError):
    """Raised when request validation fails."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str = "Validation failed",
        *,
        cause: BaseException | None = None,
        context: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        super().__init__(message, is_retryable=False, cause=cause, context=context)

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

from typing import Any, Literal

from pydantic import BaseModel, ConfigDict, Field


class RunRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request body for running an agent."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")

    input: str = Field(..., description="The input prompt for the agent")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    options: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional agent options")


class StreamRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request body for streaming agent responses."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")

    input: str = Field(..., description="The input prompt for the agent")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    options: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional agent options")


class RunResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from a run request."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    output: str = Field(..., description="The agent's response")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for the conversation")
    usage: dict[str, int] | None = Field(default=None, description="Token usage statistics")
    cost: dict[str, float] | None = Field(default=None, description="Cost information")
    metadata: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional metadata")


class StreamEvent(BaseModel):
    """An event in a streaming response."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    event: Literal["token", "update", "done", "error"] = Field(..., description="Event type")
    data: str | dict[str, Any] | None = Field(default=None, description="Event data")


class HealthResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from the health endpoint."""

    status: Literal["healthy", "unhealthy"] = Field(..., description="Health status")
    version: str = Field(..., description="Framework version")
    agent: str = Field(..., description="Agent name")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(..., description="Server uptime in seconds")


class MetricsResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from the metrics endpoint."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    requests_total: int = Field(default=0, description="Total number of requests")
    requests_success: int = Field(default=0, description="Successful requests")
    requests_failed: int = Field(default=0, description="Failed requests")
    requests_in_progress: int = Field(default=0, description="Requests currently in progress")
    average_latency_ms: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Average request latency in milliseconds")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Server uptime in seconds")


class ErrorResponse(BaseModel):
    """Standard error response."""

    error: str = Field(..., description="Error type")
    message: str = Field(..., description="Error message")
    details: dict[str, Any] | None = Field(default=None, description="Additional error details")

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

import time
from threading import Lock


class MetricsCollector:
    """Collects and provides metrics for the agent API."""

    def __init__(self) -> None:
        self._lock = Lock()
        self._start_time = time.time()
        self._requests_total = 0
        self._requests_success = 0
        self._requests_failed = 0
        self._requests_in_progress = 0
        self._total_latency_ms = 0.0

    def record_request_start(self) -> float:
        """Record the start of a request. Returns the start time."""
        with self._lock:
            self._requests_total += 1
            self._requests_in_progress += 1
        return time.time()

    def record_request_end(self, start_time: float, success: bool) -> None:
        """Record the end of a request."""
        latency_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
        with self._lock:
            self._requests_in_progress -= 1
            self._total_latency_ms += latency_ms
            if success:
                self._requests_success += 1
            else:
                self._requests_failed += 1

    def get_metrics(self) -> dict[str, float | int]:
        """Get current metrics."""
        with self._lock:
            completed = self._requests_success + self._requests_failed
            avg_latency = self._total_latency_ms / completed if completed > 0 else 0.0
            return {
                "requests_total": self._requests_total,
                "requests_success": self._requests_success,
                "requests_failed": self._requests_failed,
                "requests_in_progress": self._requests_in_progress,
                "average_latency_ms": round(avg_latency, 2),
                "uptime_seconds": round(time.time() - self._start_time, 2),
            }

    @property
    def uptime_seconds(self) -> float:
        return round(time.time() - self._start_time, 2)

    def reset(self) -> None:
        """Reset all metrics."""
        with self._lock:
            self._start_time = time.time()
            self._requests_total = 0
            self._requests_success = 0
            self._requests_failed = 0
            self._requests_in_progress = 0
            self._total_latency_ms = 0.0

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

import asyncio
import importlib.metadata
import uuid
from collections.abc import AsyncIterable
from functools import cached_property
from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

try:
    from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI, HTTPException, Request, status
    from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
    from sse_starlette.sse import EventSourceResponse, ServerSentEvent
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    raise ModuleNotFoundError(
        "Optional module [fastapi] not found.\nRun 'pip install fastapi sse-starlette' to install."
    ) from e

from beeai_framework.agents import AnyAgent, BaseAgent
from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgentSuccessEvent, ReActAgentUpdateEvent
from beeai_framework.deployment.errors import AgentExecutionError
from beeai_framework.deployment.metrics import MetricsCollector
from beeai_framework.deployment.types import (
    ErrorResponse,
    HealthResponse,
    MetricsResponse,
    RunRequest,
    RunResponse,
    StreamEvent,
    StreamRequest,
)
from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError
from beeai_framework.logger import Logger
from beeai_framework.serve import MemoryManager, init_agent_memory
from beeai_framework.serve.utils import UnlimitedMemoryManager
from beeai_framework.utils.cloneable import Cloneable
from beeai_framework.utils.strings import to_json

logger = Logger(__name__)


class AgentAPIConfig(BaseModel):
    """Configuration for the Agent API."""

    title: str = Field(default="BeeAI Agent API", description="API title")
    description: str = Field(default="Production-ready API for BeeAI agents", description="API description")
    version: str = Field(default="1.0.0", description="API version")
    docs_url: str | None = Field(default="/docs", description="OpenAPI docs URL")
    redoc_url: str | None = Field(default="/redoc", description="ReDoc URL")
    openapi_url: str | None = Field(default="/openapi.json", description="OpenAPI schema URL")
    prefix: str = Field(default="", description="API route prefix")
    api_key: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Optional API key for authentication")
    cors_origins: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list, description="CORS allowed origins")
    stateful: bool = Field(default=True, description="Whether to maintain session state")


class AgentAPI:
    """FastAPI-based API wrapper for BeeAI agents."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        agent: AnyAgent,
        *,
        config: AgentAPIConfig | None = None,
        memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        self._agent = agent
        self._config = config or AgentAPIConfig()
        self._memory_manager = memory_manager or UnlimitedMemoryManager()
        self._metrics = MetricsCollector()

        self._router = APIRouter()
        self._setup_routes()

    def _get_agent_name(self) -> str:
        """Get the agent's name."""
        if isinstance(self._agent, BaseAgent):
            return self._agent.meta.name
        return self._agent.__class__.__name__

    def _get_framework_version(self) -> str:
        """Get the BeeAI framework version."""
        try:
            return importlib.metadata.version("beeai-framework")
        except importlib.metadata.PackageNotFoundError:
            return "unknown"

    def _setup_routes(self) -> None:
        """Set up API routes."""
        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/run",
            self._handle_run,
            methods=["POST"],
            response_model=RunResponse,
            responses={400: {"model": ErrorResponse}, 500: {"model": ErrorResponse}},
            summary="Run the agent",
            description="Execute the agent with the given input and return the response.",
        )

        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/stream",
            self._handle_stream,
            methods=["POST"],
            summary="Stream agent response",
            description="Execute the agent and stream the response as server-sent events.",
        )

        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/health",
            self._handle_health,
            methods=["GET"],
            response_model=HealthResponse,
            summary="Health check",
            description="Check the health status of the API.",
        )

        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/metrics",
            self._handle_metrics,
            methods=["GET"],
            response_model=MetricsResponse,
            summary="Get metrics",
            description="Get current API metrics and statistics.",
        )

    async def _validate_api_key(self, request: Request) -> None:
        """Validate API key if configured."""
        if self._config.api_key is None:
            return

        auth_header = request.headers.get("Authorization")
        if not auth_header:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
                detail="Missing Authorization header",
            )

        if not auth_header.startswith("Bearer "):
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
                detail="Invalid Authorization header format",
            )

        token = auth_header[7:]
        if token != self._config.api_key:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
                detail="Invalid API key",
            )

    async def _handle_run(self, request: Request, body: RunRequest) -> RunResponse:
        """Handle run requests."""
        await self._validate_api_key(request)
        start_time = self._metrics.record_request_start()
        success = False

        try:
            cloned_agent = await self._agent.clone() if isinstance(self._agent, Cloneable) else self._agent
            session_id = body.session_id or str(uuid.uuid4())

            await init_agent_memory(
                cloned_agent, self._memory_manager, session_id, stateful=self._config.stateful
            )

            result = await cloned_agent.run(body.input, **body.options)

            usage = None
            cost = None

            if hasattr(result, "usage") and result.usage:
                usage = {
                    "prompt_tokens": result.usage.prompt_tokens,
                    "completion_tokens": result.usage.completion_tokens,
                    "total_tokens": result.usage.total_tokens,
                }

            if hasattr(result, "cost") and result.cost:
                cost = {
                    "prompt_tokens_usd": result.cost.prompt_tokens_usd,
                    "completion_tokens_cost_usd": result.cost.completion_tokens_cost_usd,
                    "total_cost_usd": result.cost.total_cost_usd,
                }

            success = True
            return RunResponse(
                output=result.last_message.text,
                session_id=session_id if self._config.stateful else None,
                usage=usage,
                cost=cost,
            )

        except FrameworkError as e:
            logger.error(f"Agent execution failed: {e.explain()}")
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
                detail={"error": "AgentExecutionError", "message": str(e), "details": e.context},
            )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Unexpected error: {e}")
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
                detail={"error": "InternalError", "message": str(e)},
            )
        finally:
            self._metrics.record_request_end(start_time, success)

    async def _handle_stream(self, request: Request, body: StreamRequest) -> EventSourceResponse:
        """Handle streaming requests."""
        await self._validate_api_key(request)

        async def event_generator() -> AsyncIterable[ServerSentEvent]:
            start_time = self._metrics.record_request_start()
            success = False

            try:
                cloned_agent = await self._agent.clone() if isinstance(self._agent, Cloneable) else self._agent
                session_id = body.session_id or str(uuid.uuid4())

                await init_agent_memory(
                    cloned_agent, self._memory_manager, session_id, stateful=self._config.stateful
                )

                async for data, event in cloned_agent.run(body.input, **body.options):
                    if isinstance(data, ReActAgentUpdateEvent):
                        if data.update.key == "final_answer" and data.data.final_answer is None:
                            yield ServerSentEvent(
                                data=to_json(StreamEvent(event="token", data=data.update.value).model_dump()),
                                event="token",
                            )
                        else:
                            yield ServerSentEvent(
                                data=to_json(
                                    StreamEvent(
                                        event="update",
                                        data={"key": data.update.key, "value": str(data.update.value)},
                                    ).model_dump()
                                ),
                                event="update",
                            )

                    if isinstance(data, ReActAgentSuccessEvent):
                        result_data = {
                            "output": data.data.text,
                            "iterations": len(data.iterations),
                        }
                        if session_id and self._config.stateful:
                            result_data["session_id"] = session_id

                        yield ServerSentEvent(
                            data=to_json(StreamEvent(event="done", data=result_data).model_dump()),
                            event="done",
                        )

                success = True

            except FrameworkError as e:
                logger.error(f"Stream execution failed: {e.explain()}")
                yield ServerSentEvent(
                    data=to_json(
                        StreamEvent(
                            event="error", data={"error": "AgentExecutionError", "message": str(e)}
                        ).model_dump()
                    ),
                    event="error",
                )
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Unexpected stream error: {e}")
                yield ServerSentEvent(
                    data=to_json(
                        StreamEvent(event="error", data={"error": "InternalError", "message": str(e)}).model_dump()
                    ),
                    event="error",
                )
            finally:
                self._metrics.record_request_end(start_time, success)

        return EventSourceResponse(event_generator())

    async def _handle_health(self) -> HealthResponse:
        """Handle health check requests."""
        return HealthResponse(
            status="healthy",
            version=self._get_framework_version(),
            agent=self._get_agent_name(),
            uptime_seconds=self._metrics.uptime_seconds,
        )

    async def _handle_metrics(self) -> MetricsResponse:
        """Handle metrics requests."""
        metrics = self._metrics.get_metrics()
        return MetricsResponse(**metrics)

    @cached_property
    def app(self) -> FastAPI:
        """Create and return the FastAPI application."""
        app = FastAPI(
            title=self._config.title,
            description=self._config.description,
            version=self._config.version,
            docs_url=self._config.docs_url,
            redoc_url=self._config.redoc_url,
            openapi_url=self._config.openapi_url,
        )

        if self._config.cors_origins:
            try:
                from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

                app.add_middleware(
                    CORSMiddleware,
                    allow_origins=self._config.cors_origins,
                    allow_credentials=True,
                    allow_methods=["*"],
                    allow_headers=["*"],
                )
            except ImportError:
                logger.warning("CORS middleware not available")

        app.include_router(self._router, prefix=self._config.prefix)
        return app

    @property
    def metrics(self) -> MetricsCollector:
        """Get the metrics collector."""
        return self._metrics

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

try:
    import uvicorn
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    raise ModuleNotFoundError(
        "Optional module [uvicorn] not found.\nRun 'pip install uvicorn' to install."
    ) from e

from beeai_framework.agents import AnyAgent
from beeai_framework.deployment.api import AgentAPI, AgentAPIConfig
from beeai_framework.logger import Logger
from beeai_framework.serve import MemoryManager
from beeai_framework.utils import ModelLike
from beeai_framework.utils.models import to_model

logger = Logger(__name__)


class AgentServerConfig(BaseModel):
    """Configuration for the Agent Server."""

    host: str = Field(default="0.0.0.0", description="Host to bind to")
    port: int = Field(default=8000, description="Port to bind to")
    reload: bool = Field(default=False, description="Enable auto-reload for development")
    workers: int = Field(default=1, description="Number of worker processes")
    log_level: str = Field(default="info", description="Log level for uvicorn")
    ssl_keyfile: str | None = Field(default=None, description="SSL key file path")
    ssl_certfile: str | None = Field(default=None, description="SSL certificate file path")
    api_config: AgentAPIConfig | None = Field(default=None, description="API configuration")


class AgentServer:
    """Server for hosting BeeAI agents as REST APIs."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        agent: AnyAgent,
        *,
        config: ModelLike[AgentServerConfig] | None = None,
        memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        self._agent = agent
        self._config = to_model(AgentServerConfig, config or {})
        self._memory_manager = memory_manager
        self._api = AgentAPI(
            agent,
            config=self._config.api_config,
            memory_manager=memory_manager,
        )

    @property
    def api(self) -> AgentAPI:
        """Get the underlying AgentAPI instance."""
        return self._api

    def serve(self) -> None:
        """Start the server synchronously (blocking)."""
        logger.info(f"Starting agent server on {self._config.host}:{self._config.port}")

        uvicorn_config: dict[str, Any] = {
            "host": self._config.host,
            "port": self._config.port,
            "reload": self._config.reload,
            "workers": self._config.workers if not self._config.reload else 1,
            "log_level": self._config.log_level,
        }

        if self._config.ssl_keyfile:
            uvicorn_config["ssl_keyfile"] = self._config.ssl_keyfile
        if self._config.ssl_certfile:
            uvicorn_config["ssl_certfile"] = self._config.ssl_certfile

        uvicorn.run(self._api.app, **uvicorn_config)

    async def aserve(self) -> None:
        """Start the server asynchronously."""
        logger.info(f"Starting agent server on {self._config.host}:{self._config.port}")

        config = uvicorn.Config(
            self._api.app,
            host=self._config.host,
            port=self._config.port,
            log_level=self._config.log_level,
        )

        if self._config.ssl_keyfile:
            config.ssl_keyfile = self._config.ssl_keyfile
        if self._config.ssl_certfile:
            config.ssl_certfile = self._config.ssl_certfile

        server = uvicorn.Server(config)
        await server.serve()


def serve_agent(
    agent: AnyAgent,
    *,
    host: str = "0.0.0.0",
    port: int = 8000,
    api_key: str | None = None,
    stateful: bool = True,
    memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None,
    **kwargs: Any,
) -> None:
    """
    Convenience function to serve an agent as an API.

    This is the simplest way to deploy a BeeAI agent:

        from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent
        from beeai_framework.deployment import serve_agent

        agent = ReActAgent(llm=..., tools=[], memory=...)
        serve_agent(agent, port=8000)

    Args:
        agent: The BeeAI agent to serve
        host: Host to bind to (default: 0.0.0.0)
        port: Port to bind to (default: 8000)
        api_key: Optional API key for authentication
        stateful: Whether to maintain session state (default: True)
        memory_manager: Optional memory manager for session state
        **kwargs: Additional server configuration options
    """
    api_config = AgentAPIConfig(api_key=api_key, stateful=stateful)
    server_config = AgentServerConfig(host=host, port=port, api_config=api_config, **kwargs)
    server = AgentServer(agent, config=server_config, memory_manager=memory_manager)
    server.serve()

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC

import argparse
import os
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any


def get_dockerfile_content(python_version: str = "3.11", port: int = 8000) -> str:
    """Generate Dockerfile content."""
    return f'''# BeeAI Agent Deployment Dockerfile
# Generated by beeai deploy init

FROM python:{python_version}-slim

WORKDIR /app

# Install system dependencies
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \\
    build-essential \\
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

# Copy requirements first for better caching
COPY requirements.txt .
RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt

# Copy application code
COPY . .

# Create non-root user for security
RUN useradd --create-home --shell /bin/bash appuser && \\
    chown -R appuser:appuser /app
USER appuser

# Expose the port
EXPOSE {port}

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \\
    CMD python -c "import urllib.request; urllib.request.urlopen('http://localhost:{port}/health')" || exit 1

# Run the application
CMD ["python", "serve.py"]
'''


def get_docker_compose_content(
    service_name: str = "beeai-agent",
    port: int = 8000,
    replicas: int = 1,
) -> str:
    """Generate docker-compose.yml content."""
    return f'''# BeeAI Agent Deployment Docker Compose
# Generated by beeai deploy init

services:
  {service_name}:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    ports:
      - "{port}:{port}"
    environment:
      - PORT={port}
      - PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
    restart: unless-stopped
    deploy:
      replicas: {replicas}
      resources:
        limits:
          cpus: '2'
          memory: 4G
        reservations:
          cpus: '0.5'
          memory: 1G
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "python", "-c", "import urllib.request; urllib.request.urlopen('http://localhost:{port}/health')"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s
'''


def get_requirements_content() -> str:
    """Generate requirements.txt content."""
    return '''# BeeAI Agent Requirements
# Generated by beeai deploy init

beeai-framework[watsonx-orchestrate]>=0.1.0
uvicorn>=0.27.0
'''


def get_serve_py_content(port: int = 8000) -> str:
    """Generate serve.py template content."""
    return f'''#!/usr/bin/env python
# BeeAI Agent Server
# Generated by beeai deploy init

import os
from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent
from beeai_framework.backend import ChatModel
from beeai_framework.deployment import serve_agent
from beeai_framework.memory import UnconstrainedMemory


def create_agent() -> ReActAgent:
    """Create and configure the agent."""
    # Configure your LLM - use environment variables for sensitive data
    llm = ChatModel.from_name(
        os.getenv("LLM_MODEL", "ollama:llama3.1")
    )

    # Configure your tools
    tools = []

    # Create memory
    memory = UnconstrainedMemory()

    # Create the agent
    agent = ReActAgent(
        llm=llm,
        tools=tools,
        memory=memory,
    )

    return agent


if __name__ == "__main__":
    agent = create_agent()
    port = int(os.getenv("PORT", "{port}"))
    api_key = os.getenv("API_KEY")  # Optional API key

    serve_agent(
        agent,
        host="0.0.0.0",
        port=port,
        api_key=api_key,
        stateful=True,
    )
'''


def get_env_example_content() -> str:
    """Generate .env.example content."""

# Copy this file to .env and fill in your values

# LLM Configuration
LLM_MODEL=ollama:llama3.1

# Server Configuration

# Optional API Key for authentication

def init_deployment(
    output_dir: Path,
    port: int = 8000,
    service_name: str = "beeai-agent",
    python_version: str = "3.11",
    force: bool = False,
) -> list[str]:
    """Initialize deployment files in the specified directory."""
    created_files: list[str] = []

    files: dict[str, str] = {
        "Dockerfile": get_dockerfile_content(python_version, port),
        "docker-compose.yml": get_docker_compose_content(service_name, port),
        "requirements.txt": get_requirements_content(),
        "serve.py": get_serve_py_content(port),
        ".env.example": get_env_example_content(),
        ".gitignore": get_gitignore_content(),
    }

    output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    for filename, content in files.items():
        filepath = output_dir / filename
        if filepath.exists() and not force:
            print(f"Skipping {filename} (already exists, use --force to overwrite)")
            continue

        filepath.write_text(content)
        created_files.append(filename)
        print(f"Created {filename}")

    return created_files


def main(args: list[str] | None = None) -> int:
    """Main CLI entry point."""
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        prog="beeai",
        description="BeeAI Framework CLI",
    )

    subparsers = parser.add_subparsers(dest="command", help="Available commands")

    deploy_parser = subparsers.add_parser("deploy", help="Deployment commands")
    deploy_subparsers = deploy_parser.add_subparsers(dest="deploy_command", help="Deployment sub-commands")

    init_parser = deploy_subparsers.add_parser(
        "init",
        help="Initialize deployment configuration files",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-o", "--output",
        type=Path,
        default=Path("."),
        help="Output directory (default: current directory)",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-p", "--port",
        type=int,
        default=8000,
        help="Port to expose (default: 8000)",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-n", "--name",
        type=str,
        default="beeai-agent",
        help="Service name (default: beeai-agent)",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "--python-version",
        type=str,
        default="3.11",
        help="Python version for Docker image (default: 3.11)",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-f", "--force",
        action="store_true",
        help="Overwrite existing files",
    )

    parsed = parser.parse_args(args)

    if parsed.command == "deploy" and parsed.deploy_command == "init":
        created = init_deployment(
            output_dir=parsed.output,
            port=parsed.port,
            service_name=parsed.name,
            python_version=parsed.python_version,
            force=parsed.force,
        )

        if created:
            print(f"\nCreated {len(created)} file(s) in {parsed.output}")
            print("\nNext steps:")
            print("  1. Edit serve.py to configure your agent")
            print("  2. Copy .env.example to .env and set your environment variables")
            print("  3. Build and run with: docker-compose up --build")
            print(f"  4. Access your agent at: http://localhost:{parsed.port}")
            print(f"     - POST /run       - Run the agent")
            print(f"     - POST /stream    - Stream responses")
            print(f"     - GET  /health    - Health check")
            print(f"     - GET  /metrics   - View metrics")
        return 0

    parser.print_help()
    return 1


if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

old_str
    def _to_run(
        self,
        fn: Callable[[RunContext], Awaitable[R]],
        *,
        signal: AbortSignal | None,
        run_params: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> Run[R]:
        if self._is_running:
            raise RuntimeError("Agent is already running!")

        async def handler(context: RunContext) -> R:
            try:
                self._is_running = True
                return await fn(context)
            except Exception as e:
                raise AgentError.ensure(e)
            finally:
                self._is_running = False

        return RunContext.enter(
            self,
            handler,
            signal=signal,
            run_params=run_params,
        ).middleware(*self.middlewares)


AnyAgent = BaseAgent[Any]
new_str
    def _to_run(
        self,
        fn: Callable[[RunContext], Awaitable[R]],
        *,
        signal: AbortSignal | None,
        run_params: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> Run[R]:
        if self._is_running:
            raise RuntimeError("Agent is already running!")

        async def handler(context: RunContext) -> R:
            try:
                self._is_running = True
                return await fn(context)
            except Exception as e:
                raise AgentError.ensure(e)
            finally:
                self._is_running = False

        return RunContext.enter(
            self,
            handler,
            signal=signal,
            run_params=run_params,
        ).middleware(*self.middlewares)

    def serve(
        self,
        *,
        host: str = "0.0.0.0",
        port: int = 8000,
        api_key: str | None = None,
        stateful: bool = True,
        memory_manager: "MemoryManager | None" = None,
        **kwargs: Any,
    ) -> None:
        """
        Serve this agent as a production-ready API.

        This method starts a FastAPI server that exposes the agent via REST endpoints:
        - POST /run    - Execute the agent and return the response
        - POST /stream - Stream the agent's response as server-sent events
        - GET  /health - Health check endpoint
        - GET  /metrics - Metrics and statistics

        Example:
            agent = ReActAgent(llm=..., tools=[], memory=...)
            agent.serve(port=8000)

        Args:
            host: Host to bind to (default: 0.0.0.0)
            port: Port to bind to (default: 8000)
            api_key: Optional API key for authentication
            stateful: Whether to maintain session state across requests (default: True)
            memory_manager: Optional memory manager for session state
            **kwargs: Additional server configuration options
        """
        from beeai_framework.deployment import serve_agent

        serve_agent(
            self,
            host=host,
            port=port,
            api_key=api_key,
            stateful=stateful,
            memory_manager=memory_manager,
            **kwargs,
        )

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

import pytest

from beeai_framework.deployment.types import (
    ErrorResponse,
    HealthResponse,
    MetricsResponse,
    RunRequest,
    RunResponse,
    StreamEvent,
    StreamRequest,
)


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestRunRequest:
    def test_minimal_request(self) -> None:
        request = RunRequest(input="Hello")
        assert request.input == "Hello"
        assert request.session_id is None
        assert request.options == {}

    def test_full_request(self) -> None:
        request = RunRequest(
            input="Hello",
            session_id="session-123",
            options={"max_iterations": 5},
        )
        assert request.input == "Hello"
        assert request.session_id == "session-123"
        assert request.options == {"max_iterations": 5}


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestStreamRequest:
    def test_minimal_request(self) -> None:
        request = StreamRequest(input="Hello")
        assert request.input == "Hello"
        assert request.session_id is None

    def test_with_session(self) -> None:
        request = StreamRequest(input="Hello", session_id="sess-1")
        assert request.session_id == "sess-1"


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestRunResponse:
    def test_minimal_response(self) -> None:
        response = RunResponse(output="World")
        assert response.output == "World"
        assert response.session_id is None
        assert response.usage is None
        assert response.metadata == {}

    def test_full_response(self) -> None:
        response = RunResponse(
            output="World",
            session_id="sess-1",
            usage={"prompt_tokens": 10, "completion_tokens": 5, "total_tokens": 15},
            cost={"total_cost_usd": 0.001},
            metadata={"model": "gpt-4"},
        )
        assert response.output == "World"
        assert response.usage["total_tokens"] == 15
        assert response.cost["total_cost_usd"] == 0.001


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestStreamEvent:
    def test_token_event(self) -> None:
        event = StreamEvent(event="token", data="Hello")
        assert event.event == "token"
        assert event.data == "Hello"

    def test_done_event(self) -> None:
        event = StreamEvent(event="done", data={"output": "Complete"})
        assert event.event == "done"
        assert event.data["output"] == "Complete"

    def test_error_event(self) -> None:
        event = StreamEvent(event="error", data={"message": "Failed"})
        assert event.event == "error"


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestHealthResponse:
    def test_health_response(self) -> None:
        response = HealthResponse(
            status="healthy",
            version="0.1.0",
            agent="TestAgent",
            uptime_seconds=123.45,
        )
        assert response.status == "healthy"
        assert response.version == "0.1.0"
        assert response.agent == "TestAgent"
        assert response.uptime_seconds == 123.45


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestMetricsResponse:
    def test_default_metrics(self) -> None:
        response = MetricsResponse()
        assert response.requests_total == 0
        assert response.requests_success == 0
        assert response.requests_failed == 0
        assert response.requests_in_progress == 0
        assert response.average_latency_ms == 0.0

    def test_custom_metrics(self) -> None:
        response = MetricsResponse(
            requests_total=100,
            requests_success=95,
            requests_failed=5,
            average_latency_ms=150.5,
        )
        assert response.requests_total == 100
        assert response.requests_success == 95


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestErrorResponse:
    def test_error_response(self) -> None:
        response = ErrorResponse(
            error="ValidationError",
            message="Invalid input",
            details={"field": "input"},
        )
        assert response.error == "ValidationError"
        assert response.message == "Invalid input"
        assert response.details["field"] == "input"

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

import time

import pytest

from beeai_framework.deployment.metrics import MetricsCollector


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestMetricsCollector:
    def test_initial_state(self) -> None:
        collector = MetricsCollector()
        metrics = collector.get_metrics()

        assert metrics["requests_total"] == 0
        assert metrics["requests_success"] == 0
        assert metrics["requests_failed"] == 0
        assert metrics["requests_in_progress"] == 0
        assert metrics["average_latency_ms"] == 0.0
        assert metrics["uptime_seconds"] >= 0

    def test_record_successful_request(self) -> None:
        collector = MetricsCollector()

        start_time = collector.record_request_start()
        time.sleep(0.01)
        collector.record_request_end(start_time, success=True)

        metrics = collector.get_metrics()
        assert metrics["requests_total"] == 1
        assert metrics["requests_success"] == 1
        assert metrics["requests_failed"] == 0
        assert metrics["requests_in_progress"] == 0
        assert metrics["average_latency_ms"] >= 10

    def test_record_failed_request(self) -> None:
        collector = MetricsCollector()

        start_time = collector.record_request_start()
        collector.record_request_end(start_time, success=False)

        metrics = collector.get_metrics()
        assert metrics["requests_total"] == 1
        assert metrics["requests_success"] == 0
        assert metrics["requests_failed"] == 1

    def test_concurrent_requests(self) -> None:
        collector = MetricsCollector()

        start1 = collector.record_request_start()
        start2 = collector.record_request_start()

        metrics = collector.get_metrics()
        assert metrics["requests_in_progress"] == 2

        collector.record_request_end(start1, success=True)
        metrics = collector.get_metrics()
        assert metrics["requests_in_progress"] == 1

        collector.record_request_end(start2, success=True)
        metrics = collector.get_metrics()
        assert metrics["requests_in_progress"] == 0

    def test_average_latency(self) -> None:
        collector = MetricsCollector()

        for _ in range(3):
            start = collector.record_request_start()
            time.sleep(0.01)
            collector.record_request_end(start, success=True)

        metrics = collector.get_metrics()
        assert metrics["average_latency_ms"] >= 10

    def test_reset(self) -> None:
        collector = MetricsCollector()

        start = collector.record_request_start()
        collector.record_request_end(start, success=True)

        collector.reset()
        metrics = collector.get_metrics()

        assert metrics["requests_total"] == 0
        assert metrics["requests_success"] == 0
        assert metrics["uptime_seconds"] < 1

    def test_uptime_property(self) -> None:
        collector = MetricsCollector()
        time.sleep(0.05)
        assert collector.uptime_seconds >= 0.05

    main,
)

@pytest.mark.unit
class TestInitDeployment:
    def test_creates_all_files(self) -> None:
        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
            output_dir = Path(tmpdir)
            created = init_deployment(output_dir)

            assert "Dockerfile" in created
            assert "docker-compose.yml" in created
            assert "requirements.txt" in created
            assert "serve.py" in created
            assert ".env.example" in created
            assert ".gitignore" in created

            for filename in created:
                assert (output_dir / filename).exists()

    def test_skips_existing_files(self, capsys: pytest.CaptureFixture[str]) -> None:
        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
            output_dir = Path(tmpdir)

            (output_dir / "Dockerfile").write_text("existing")
            created = init_deployment(output_dir)

            assert "Dockerfile" not in created
            assert (output_dir / "Dockerfile").read_text() == "existing"

    def test_force_overwrites(self) -> None:
        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
            output_dir = Path(tmpdir)

            (output_dir / "Dockerfile").write_text("existing")
            created = init_deployment(output_dir, force=True)

            assert "Dockerfile" in created
            assert (output_dir / "Dockerfile").read_text() != "existing"

    def test_custom_port(self) -> None:
        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
            output_dir = Path(tmpdir)
            init_deployment(output_dir, port=9000)

            dockerfile_content = (output_dir / "Dockerfile").read_text()
            assert "EXPOSE 9000" in dockerfile_content


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestCLI:
    def test_deploy_init_command(self) -> None:
        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
            result = main(["deploy", "init", "-o", tmpdir])
            assert result == 0
            assert (Path(tmpdir) / "Dockerfile").exists()

    def test_deploy_init_with_options(self) -> None:
        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
            result = main([
                "deploy", "init",
                "-o", tmpdir,
                "-p", "9000",
                "-n", "custom-agent",
                "--python-version", "3.12",
            ])
            assert result == 0

            dockerfile = (Path(tmpdir) / "Dockerfile").read_text()
            assert "EXPOSE 9000" in dockerfile
            assert "python:3.12" in dockerfile

    def test_no_command_shows_help(self) -> None:
        result = main([])
        assert result == 1

    def test_help_exits_cleanly(self) -> None:
        with pytest.raises(SystemExit) as exc:
            main(["--help"])
        assert exc.value.code == 0

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

import pytest

from beeai_framework.deployment.errors import (
    AgentExecutionError,
    DeploymentError,
    ValidationError,
)
from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestDeploymentError:
    def test_inherits_framework_error(self) -> None:
        error = DeploymentError("test error")
        assert isinstance(error, FrameworkError)
        assert error.message == "test error"

    def test_default_properties(self) -> None:
        error = DeploymentError()
        assert error.fatal is False
        assert error.retryable is True

    def test_with_context(self) -> None:
        error = DeploymentError("test", context={"key": "value"})
        assert error.context == {"key": "value"}


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestAgentExecutionError:
    def test_inherits_deployment_error(self) -> None:
        error = AgentExecutionError("execution failed")
        assert isinstance(error, DeploymentError)

    def test_with_cause(self) -> None:
        cause = ValueError("original error")
        error = AgentExecutionError("execution failed", cause=cause)
        assert error.__cause__ is cause


@pytest.mark.unit
class TestValidationError:
    def test_not_retryable(self) -> None:
        error = ValidationError("invalid input")
        assert error.retryable is False

    def test_with_details(self) -> None:
        error = ValidationError(
            "validation failed",
            context={"field": "input", "reason": "empty"},
        )
        assert error.context["field"] == "input"

"""
Example: Serving a BeeAI Agent as a Production API

This example demonstrates multiple ways to deploy a BeeAI agent:
1. Using agent.serve() method
2. Using serve_agent() function
3. Using AgentServer for more control
"""

import os

from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent
from beeai_framework.backend import ChatModel
from beeai_framework.deployment import AgentServer, AgentServerConfig, serve_agent
from beeai_framework.deployment.api import AgentAPIConfig
from beeai_framework.memory import UnconstrainedMemory
from beeai_framework.serve.utils import LRUMemoryManager
from beeai_framework.tools.weather import OpenMeteoTool


def create_agent() -> ReActAgent:
    """Create a sample agent with weather tool."""
    llm = ChatModel.from_name(os.getenv("LLM_MODEL", "ollama:llama3.1"))

    agent = ReActAgent(
        llm=llm,
        tools=[OpenMeteoTool()],
        memory=UnconstrainedMemory(),
    )

    return agent


def example_simple_serve() -> None:
    """Simplest way: use agent.serve() method."""
    agent = create_agent()

    # Start serving - this will block and run the server
    agent.serve(port=8000)


def example_serve_function() -> None:
    """Using the serve_agent convenience function."""
    agent = create_agent()

    serve_agent(
        agent,
        host="0.0.0.0",
        port=8000,
        api_key=os.getenv("API_KEY"),
        stateful=True,
    )


def example_agent_server() -> None:
    """Using AgentServer for more configuration options."""
    agent = create_agent()

    # Configure API settings
    api_config = AgentAPIConfig(
        title="My Weather Agent API",
        description="An agent that can check the weather",
        api_key=os.getenv("API_KEY"),
        cors_origins=["http://localhost:3000"],
        stateful=True,
    )

    # Configure server settings
    server_config = AgentServerConfig(
        host="0.0.0.0",
        port=8000,
        workers=1,
        log_level="info",
        api_config=api_config,
    )

    # Use LRU memory manager for bounded session storage
    memory_manager = LRUMemoryManager(maxsize=100)

    server = AgentServer(
        agent,
        config=server_config,
        memory_manager=memory_manager,
    )

    server.serve()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    import sys

    mode = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else "simple"

    if mode == "simple":
        example_simple_serve()
    elif mode == "function":
        example_serve_function()
    elif mode == "server":
        example_agent_server()
    else:
        print(f"Unknown mode: {mode}")
        print("Usage: python deployment.py [simple|function|server]")
        sys.exit(1)

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

from typing import TYPE_CHECKING


def __getattr__(name: str) -> object:
    """Lazy imports for optional dependencies."""
    if name in ("AgentAPI", "AgentAPIConfig"):
        from beeai_framework.deployment.api import AgentAPI, AgentAPIConfig
        return AgentAPI if name == "AgentAPI" else AgentAPIConfig

    if name in ("AgentServer", "AgentServerConfig", "serve_agent"):
        from beeai_framework.deployment.server import AgentServer, AgentServerConfig, serve_agent
        if name == "AgentServer":
            return AgentServer
        elif name == "AgentServerConfig":
            return AgentServerConfig
        else:
            return serve_agent

    raise AttributeError(f"module {__name__!r} has no attribute {name!r}")


if TYPE_CHECKING:
    from beeai_framework.deployment.api import AgentAPI, AgentAPIConfig
    from beeai_framework.deployment.server import AgentServer, AgentServerConfig, serve_agent

__all__ = [
    "AgentAPI",
    "AgentAPIConfig",
    "AgentServer",
    "AgentServerConfig",
    "serve_agent",
]

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Literal

from pydantic import BaseModel, ConfigDict, Field


class RunRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request body for running an agent."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")

    input: str = Field(..., description="The input prompt for the agent")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    options: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional agent options")


class StreamRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request body for streaming agent responses."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")

    input: str = Field(..., description="The input prompt for the agent")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    options: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional agent options")


class RunResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from a run request."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    output: str = Field(..., description="The agent's response")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for the conversation")
    usage: dict[str, int] | None = Field(default=None, description="Token usage statistics")
    cost: dict[str, float] | None = Field(default=None, description="Cost information")
    metadata: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional metadata")


class StreamEvent(BaseModel):
    """An event in a streaming response."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    event: Literal["token", "update", "done", "error"] = Field(..., description="Event type")
    data: str | dict[str, Any] | None = Field(default=None, description="Event data")


class HealthResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from the health endpoint."""

    status: Literal["healthy", "unhealthy"] = Field(..., description="Health status")
    version: str = Field(..., description="Framework version")
    agent: str = Field(..., description="Agent name")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(..., description="Server uptime in seconds")


class MetricsResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from the metrics endpoint."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    requests_total: int = Field(default=0, description="Total number of requests")
    requests_success: int = Field(default=0, description="Successful requests")
    requests_failed: int = Field(default=0, description="Failed requests")
    requests_in_progress: int = Field(default=0, description="Requests currently in progress")
    average_latency_ms: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Average request latency in milliseconds")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Server uptime in seconds")


class ErrorResponse(BaseModel):
    """Standard error response."""

    error: str = Field(..., description="Error type")
    message: str = Field(..., description="Error message")
    details: dict[str, Any] | None = Field(default=None, description="Additional error details")

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

from typing import Any, Dict, Literal, Optional, Union

from pydantic import BaseModel, ConfigDict, Field


class RunRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request body for running an agent."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")

    input: str = Field(..., description="The input prompt for the agent")
    session_id: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    options: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional agent options")


class StreamRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request body for streaming agent responses."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")

    input: str = Field(..., description="The input prompt for the agent")
    session_id: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    options: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional agent options")


class RunResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from a run request."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    output: str = Field(..., description="The agent's response")
    session_id: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for the conversation")
    usage: Optional[Dict[str, int]] = Field(default=None, description="Token usage statistics")
    cost: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = Field(default=None, description="Cost information")
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional metadata")


class StreamEvent(BaseModel):
    """An event in a streaming response."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    event: Literal["token", "update", "done", "error"] = Field(..., description="Event type")
    data: Optional[Union[str, Dict[str, Any]]] = Field(default=None, description="Event data")


class HealthResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from the health endpoint."""

    status: Literal["healthy", "unhealthy"] = Field(..., description="Health status")
    version: str = Field(..., description="Framework version")
    agent: str = Field(..., description="Agent name")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(..., description="Server uptime in seconds")


class MetricsResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response from the metrics endpoint."""

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow")

    requests_total: int = Field(default=0, description="Total number of requests")
    requests_success: int = Field(default=0, description="Successful requests")
    requests_failed: int = Field(default=0, description="Failed requests")
    requests_in_progress: int = Field(default=0, description="Requests currently in progress")
    average_latency_ms: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Average request latency in milliseconds")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Server uptime in seconds")


class ErrorResponse(BaseModel):
    """Standard error response."""

    error: str = Field(..., description="Error type")
    message: str = Field(..., description="Error message")
    details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = Field(default=None, description="Additional error details")

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

import asyncio
import importlib.metadata
import uuid
from collections.abc import AsyncIterable
from functools import cached_property
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

try:
    from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI, HTTPException, Request, status
    from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
    from sse_starlette.sse import EventSourceResponse, ServerSentEvent
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    raise ModuleNotFoundError(
        "Optional module [fastapi] not found.\nRun 'pip install fastapi sse-starlette' to install."
    ) from e

from beeai_framework.agents import AnyAgent, BaseAgent
from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgentSuccessEvent, ReActAgentUpdateEvent
from beeai_framework.deployment.errors import AgentExecutionError
from beeai_framework.deployment.metrics import MetricsCollector
from beeai_framework.deployment.types import (
    ErrorResponse,
    HealthResponse,
    MetricsResponse,
    RunRequest,
    RunResponse,
    StreamEvent,
    StreamRequest,
)
from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError
from beeai_framework.logger import Logger
from beeai_framework.serve import MemoryManager, init_agent_memory
from beeai_framework.serve.utils import UnlimitedMemoryManager
from beeai_framework.utils.cloneable import Cloneable
from beeai_framework.utils.strings import to_json

logger = Logger(__name__)


class AgentAPIConfig(BaseModel):
    """Configuration for the Agent API."""

    title: str = Field(default="BeeAI Agent API", description="API title")
    description: str = Field(default="Production-ready API for BeeAI agents", description="API description")
    version: str = Field(default="1.0.0", description="API version")
    docs_url: Optional[str] = Field(default="/docs", description="OpenAPI docs URL")
    redoc_url: Optional[str] = Field(default="/redoc", description="ReDoc URL")
    openapi_url: Optional[str] = Field(default="/openapi.json", description="OpenAPI schema URL")
    prefix: str = Field(default="", description="API route prefix")
    api_key: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, description="Optional API key for authentication")
    cors_origins: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list, description="CORS allowed origins")
    stateful: bool = Field(default=True, description="Whether to maintain session state")


class AgentAPI:
    """FastAPI-based API wrapper for BeeAI agents."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        agent: AnyAgent,
        *,
        config: Optional[AgentAPIConfig] = None,
        memory_manager: Optional[MemoryManager] = None,
    ) -> None:
        self._agent = agent
        self._config = config or AgentAPIConfig()
        self._memory_manager = memory_manager or UnlimitedMemoryManager()
        self._metrics = MetricsCollector()

        self._router = APIRouter()
        self._setup_routes()

    def _get_agent_name(self) -> str:
        """Get the agent's name."""
        if isinstance(self._agent, BaseAgent):
            return self._agent.meta.name
        return self._agent.__class__.__name__

    def _get_framework_version(self) -> str:
        """Get the BeeAI framework version."""
        try:
            return importlib.metadata.version("beeai-framework")
        except importlib.metadata.PackageNotFoundError:
            return "unknown"

    def _setup_routes(self) -> None:
        """Set up API routes."""
        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/run",
            self._handle_run,
            methods=["POST"],
            response_model=RunResponse,
            responses={400: {"model": ErrorResponse}, 500: {"model": ErrorResponse}},
            summary="Run the agent",
            description="Execute the agent with the given input and return the response.",
        )

        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/stream",
            self._handle_stream,
            methods=["POST"],
            summary="Stream agent response",
            description="Execute the agent and stream the response as server-sent events.",
        )

        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/health",
            self._handle_health,
            methods=["GET"],
            response_model=HealthResponse,
            summary="Health check",
            description="Check the health status of the API.",
        )

        self._router.add_api_route(
            "/metrics",
            self._handle_metrics,
            methods=["GET"],
            response_model=MetricsResponse,
            summary="Get metrics",
            description="Get current API metrics and statistics.",
        )

    async def _validate_api_key(self, request: Request) -> None:
        """Validate API key if configured."""
        if self._config.api_key is None:
            return

        auth_header = request.headers.get("Authorization")
        if not auth_header:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
                detail="Missing Authorization header",
            )

        if not auth_header.startswith("Bearer "):
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
                detail="Invalid Authorization header format",
            )

        token = auth_header[7:]
        if token != self._config.api_key:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
                detail="Invalid API key",
            )

    async def _handle_run(self, request: Request, body: RunRequest) -> RunResponse:
        """Handle run requests."""
        await self._validate_api_key(request)
        start_time = self._metrics.record_request_start()
        success = False

        try:
            cloned_agent = await self._agent.clone() if isinstance(self._agent, Cloneable) else self._agent
            session_id = body.session_id or str(uuid.uuid4())

            await init_agent_memory(
                cloned_agent, self._memory_manager, session_id, stateful=self._config.stateful
            )

            result = await cloned_agent.run(body.input, **body.options)

            usage: Optional[Dict[str, int]] = None
            cost: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = None

            if hasattr(result, "usage") and result.usage:
                usage = {
                    "prompt_tokens": result.usage.prompt_tokens,
                    "completion_tokens": result.usage.completion_tokens,
                    "total_tokens": result.usage.total_tokens,
                }

            if hasattr(result, "cost") and result.cost:
                cost = {
                    "prompt_tokens_usd": result.cost.prompt_tokens_usd,
                    "completion_tokens_cost_usd": result.cost.completion_tokens_cost_usd,
                    "total_cost_usd": result.cost.total_cost_usd,
                }

            success = True
            return RunResponse(
                output=result.last_message.text,
                session_id=session_id if self._config.stateful else None,
                usage=usage,
                cost=cost,
            )

        except FrameworkError as e:
            logger.error(f"Agent execution failed: {e.explain()}")
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
                detail={"error": "AgentExecutionError", "message": str(e), "details": e.context},
            )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Unexpected error: {e}")
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
                detail={"error": "InternalError", "message": str(e)},
            )
        finally:
            self._metrics.record_request_end(start_time, success)

    async def _handle_stream(self, request: Request, body: StreamRequest) -> EventSourceResponse:
        """Handle streaming requests."""
        await self._validate_api_key(request)

        async def event_generator() -> AsyncIterable[ServerSentEvent]:
            start_time = self._metrics.record_request_start()
            success = False

            try:
                cloned_agent = await self._agent.clone() if isinstance(self._agent, Cloneable) else self._agent
                session_id = body.session_id or str(uuid.uuid4())

                await init_agent_memory(
                    cloned_agent, self._memory_manager, session_id, stateful=self._config.stateful
                )

                async for data, event in cloned_agent.run(body.input, **body.options):
                    if isinstance(data, ReActAgentUpdateEvent):
                        if data.update.key == "final_answer" and data.data.final_answer is None:
                            yield ServerSentEvent(
                                data=to_json(StreamEvent(event="token", data=data.update.value).model_dump()),
                                event="token",
                            )
                        else:
                            yield ServerSentEvent(
                                data=to_json(
                                    StreamEvent(
                                        event="update",
                                        data={"key": data.update.key, "value": str(data.update.value)},
                                    ).model_dump()
                                ),
                                event="update",
                            )

                    if isinstance(data, ReActAgentSuccessEvent):
                        result_data: Dict[str, Any] = {
                            "output": data.data.text,
                            "iterations": len(data.iterations),
                        }
                        if session_id and self._config.stateful:
                            result_data["session_id"] = session_id

                        yield ServerSentEvent(
                            data=to_json(StreamEvent(event="done", data=result_data).model_dump()),
                            event="done",
                        )

                success = True

            except FrameworkError as e:
                logger.error(f"Stream execution failed: {e.explain()}")
                yield ServerSentEvent(
                    data=to_json(
                        StreamEvent(
                            event="error", data={"error": "AgentExecutionError", "message": str(e)}
                        ).model_dump()
                    ),
                    event="error",
                )
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Unexpected stream error: {e}")
                yield ServerSentEvent(
                    data=to_json(
                        StreamEvent(event="error", data={"error": "InternalError", "message": str(e)}).model_dump()
                    ),
                    event="error",
                )
            finally:
                self._metrics.record_request_end(start_time, success)

        return EventSourceResponse(event_generator())

    async def _handle_health(self) -> HealthResponse:
        """Handle health check requests."""
        return HealthResponse(
            status="healthy",
            version=self._get_framework_version(),
            agent=self._get_agent_name(),
            uptime_seconds=self._metrics.uptime_seconds,
        )

    async def _handle_metrics(self) -> MetricsResponse:
        """Handle metrics requests."""
        metrics = self._metrics.get_metrics()
        return MetricsResponse(**metrics)

    @cached_property
    def app(self) -> FastAPI:
        """Create and return the FastAPI application."""
        app = FastAPI(
            title=self._config.title,
            description=self._config.description,
            version=self._config.version,
            docs_url=self._config.docs_url,
            redoc_url=self._config.redoc_url,
            openapi_url=self._config.openapi_url,
        )

        if self._config.cors_origins:
            try:
                from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

                app.add_middleware(
                    CORSMiddleware,
                    allow_origins=self._config.cors_origins,
                    allow_credentials=True,
                    allow_methods=["*"],
                    allow_headers=["*"],
                )
            except ImportError:
                logger.warning("CORS middleware not available")

        app.include_router(self._router, prefix=self._config.prefix)
        return app

    @property
    def metrics(self) -> MetricsCollector:
        """Get the metrics collector."""
        return self._metrics
