# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

from typing import Any, Optional

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

try:
    import uvicorn
except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
    raise ModuleNotFoundError(
        "Optional module [uvicorn] not found.\nRun 'pip install uvicorn' to install."
    ) from e

from beeai_framework.agents import AnyAgent
from beeai_framework.deployment.api import AgentAPI, AgentAPIConfig
from beeai_framework.logger import Logger
from beeai_framework.serve import MemoryManager
from beeai_framework.utils import ModelLike
from beeai_framework.utils.models import to_model

logger = Logger(__name__)


class AgentServerConfig(BaseModel):
    """Configuration for the Agent Server."""

    host: str = Field(default="0.0.0.0", description="Host to bind to")
    port: int = Field(default=8000, description="Port to bind to")
    reload: bool = Field(default=False, description="Enable auto-reload for development")
    workers: int = Field(default=1, description="Number of worker processes")
    log_level: str = Field(default="info", description="Log level for uvicorn")
    ssl_keyfile: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, description="SSL key file path")
    ssl_certfile: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, description="SSL certificate file path")
    api_config: Optional[AgentAPIConfig] = Field(default=None, description="API configuration")


class AgentServer:
    """Server for hosting BeeAI agents as REST APIs."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        agent: AnyAgent,
        *,
        config: Optional[ModelLike[AgentServerConfig]] = None,
        memory_manager: Optional[MemoryManager] = None,
    ) -> None:
        self._agent = agent
        self._config = to_model(AgentServerConfig, config or {})
        self._memory_manager = memory_manager
        self._api = AgentAPI(
            agent,
            config=self._config.api_config,
            memory_manager=memory_manager,
        )

    @property
    def api(self) -> AgentAPI:
        """Get the underlying AgentAPI instance."""
        return self._api

    def serve(self) -> None:
        """Start the server synchronously (blocking)."""
        logger.info(f"Starting agent server on {self._config.host}:{self._config.port}")

        uvicorn_config: dict[str, Any] = {
            "host": self._config.host,
            "port": self._config.port,
            "reload": self._config.reload,
            "workers": self._config.workers if not self._config.reload else 1,
            "log_level": self._config.log_level,
        }

        if self._config.ssl_keyfile:
            uvicorn_config["ssl_keyfile"] = self._config.ssl_keyfile
        if self._config.ssl_certfile:
            uvicorn_config["ssl_certfile"] = self._config.ssl_certfile

        uvicorn.run(self._api.app, **uvicorn_config)

    async def aserve(self) -> None:
        """Start the server asynchronously."""
        logger.info(f"Starting agent server on {self._config.host}:{self._config.port}")

        config = uvicorn.Config(
            self._api.app,
            host=self._config.host,
            port=self._config.port,
            log_level=self._config.log_level,
        )

        if self._config.ssl_keyfile:
            config.ssl_keyfile = self._config.ssl_keyfile
        if self._config.ssl_certfile:
            config.ssl_certfile = self._config.ssl_certfile

        server = uvicorn.Server(config)
        await server.serve()


def serve_agent(
    agent: AnyAgent,
    *,
    host: str = "0.0.0.0",
    port: int = 8000,
    api_key: Optional[str] = None,
    stateful: bool = True,
    memory_manager: Optional[MemoryManager] = None,
    **kwargs: Any,
) -> None:
    """
    Convenience function to serve an agent as an API.

    This is the simplest way to deploy a BeeAI agent:

        from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent
        from beeai_framework.deployment import serve_agent

        agent = ReActAgent(llm=..., tools=[], memory=...)
        serve_agent(agent, port=8000)

    Args:
        agent: The BeeAI agent to serve
        host: Host to bind to (default: 0.0.0.0)
        port: Port to bind to (default: 8000)
        api_key: Optional API key for authentication
        stateful: Whether to maintain session state (default: True)
        memory_manager: Optional memory manager for session state
        **kwargs: Additional server configuration options
    """
    api_config = AgentAPIConfig(api_key=api_key, stateful=stateful)
    server_config = AgentServerConfig(host=host, port=port, api_config=api_config, **kwargs)
    server = AgentServer(agent, config=server_config, memory_manager=memory_manager)
    server.serve()

166 ) 167 168 result = await cloned_agent.run(body.input, **body.options) 169 170 usage: Optional[Dict[str, int]] = None 171 cost: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = None 172 173 if hasattr(result, "usage") and result.usage: 174 usage = { 175 "prompt_tokens": result.usage.prompt_tokens, 176 "completion_tokens": result.usage.completion_tokens, 177 "total_tokens": result.usage.total_tokens, 178 } 179 180 if hasattr(result, "cost") and result.cost: 181 cost = { 182 "prompt_tokens_usd": result.cost.prompt_tokens_usd, 183 "completion_tokens_cost_usd": result.cost.completion_tokens_cost_usd, 184 "total_cost_usd": result.cost.total_cost_usd, 185 } 186 187 success = True 188 return RunResponse( 189 output=result.last_message.text, 190 session_id=session_id if self._config.stateful else None, 191 usage=usage, 192 cost=cost, 193 ) 194 195 except FrameworkError as e: 196 logger.error(f"Agent execution failed: {e.explain()}") 197 raise HTTPException( 198 status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, 199 detail={"error": "AgentExecutionError", "message": str(e), "details": e.context}, 200 ) 201 except Exception as e: 202 logger.error(f"Unexpected error: {e}") 203 raise HTTPException( 204 status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, 205 detail={"error": "InternalError", "message": str(e)}, 206 ) 207 finally: 208 self._metrics.record_request_end(start_time, success) 209 210 async def _handle_stream(self, request: Request, body: StreamRequest) -> EventSourceResponse: 211 """Handle streaming requests.""" 212 await self._validate_api_key(request) 213 214 async def event_generator() -> AsyncIterable[ServerSentEvent]: 215 start_time = self._metrics.record_request_start() 216 success = False 217 218 try: 219 cloned_agent = await self._agent.clone() if isinstance(self._agent, Cloneable) else self._agent 220 session_id = body.session_id or str(uuid.uuid4()) 221 222 await init_agent_memory( 223 cloned_agent, self._memory_manager, session_id, stateful=self._config.stateful 224 ) 225 226 async for data, event in cloned_agent.run(body.input, **body.options): 227 if isinstance(data, ReActAgentUpdateEvent): 228 if data.update.key == "final_answer" and data.data.final_answer is None: 229 yield ServerSentEvent( 230 data=to_json(StreamEvent(event="token", data=data.update.value).model_dump()), 231 event="token", 232 ) 233 else: 234 yield ServerSentEvent( 235 data=to_json( 236 StreamEvent( 237 event="update", 238 data={"key": data.update.key, "value": str(data.update.value)}, 239 ).model_dump() 240 ), 241 event="update", 242 ) 243 244 if isinstance(data, ReActAgentSuccessEvent): 245 result_data: Dict[str, Any] = { 246 "output": data.data.text, 247 "iterations": len(data.iterations), 248 } 249 if session_id and self._config.stateful: 250 result_data["session_id"] = session_id 251 252 yield ServerSentEvent( 253 data=to_json(StreamEvent(event="done", data=result_data).model_dump()), 254 event="done", 255 ) 256 257 success = True 258 259 except FrameworkError as e: 260 logger.error(f"Stream execution failed: {e.explain()}") 261 yield ServerSentEvent( 262 data=to_json( 263 StreamEvent( 264 event="error", data={"error": "AgentExecutionError", "message": str(e)} 265 ).model_dump() 266 ), 267 event="error", 268 ) 269 except Exception as e: 270 logger.error(f"Unexpected stream error: {e}") 271 yield ServerSentEvent( 272 data=to_json( 273 StreamEvent(event="error", data={"error": "InternalError", "message": str(e)}).model_dump() 274 ), 275 event="error", 276 ) 277 finally: 278 self._metrics.record_request_end(start_time, success) 279 280 return EventSourceResponse(event_generator()) 281 282 async def _handle_health(self) -> HealthResponse: 283 """Handle health check requests.""" 284 return HealthResponse( 285 status="healthy", 286 version=self._get_framework_version(), 287 agent=self._get_agent_name(), 288 uptime_seconds=self._metrics.uptime_seconds, 289 ) 290 291 async def _handle_metrics(self) -> MetricsResponse: 292 """Handle metrics requests.""" 293 metrics = self._metrics.get_metrics() 294 return MetricsResponse(**metrics) 295 296 @cached_property 297 def app(self) -> FastAPI: 298 """Create and return the FastAPI application.""" 299 app = FastAPI( 300 title=self._config.title, 301 description=self._config.description, 302 version=self._config.version, 303 docs_url=self._config.docs_url, 304 redoc_url=self._config.redoc_url, 305 openapi_url=self._config.openapi_url, 306 ) 307 308 if self._config.cors_origins: 309 try: 310 from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware 311 312 app.add_middleware( 313 CORSMiddleware, 314 allow_origins=self._config.cors_origins, 315 allow_credentials=True, 316 allow_methods=["*"], 317 allow_headers=["*"], 318 ) 319 except ImportError: 320 logger.warning("CORS middleware not available") 321 322 app.include_router(self._router, prefix=self._config.prefix) 323 return app 324 325 @property 326 def metrics(self) -> MetricsCollector: 327 """Get the metrics collector.""" 328 return self._metrics 329

1 """ 2 Example: Serving a BeeAI Agent as a Production API 3 4 This example demonstrates multiple ways to deploy a BeeAI agent: 5 1. Using agent.serve() method 6 2. Using serve_agent() function 7 3. Using AgentServer for more control 8 """ 9 10 import os 11 12 from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent 13 from beeai_framework.backend import ChatModel 14 from beeai_framework.deployment import AgentServer, AgentServerConfig, serve_agent 15 from beeai_framework.deployment.api import AgentAPIConfig 16 from beeai_framework.memory import UnconstrainedMemory 17 from beeai_framework.serve.utils import LRUMemoryManager 18 from beeai_framework.tools.weather import OpenMeteoTool 19 20 21 def create_agent() -> ReActAgent: 22 """Create a sample agent with weather tool.""" 23 llm = ChatModel.from_name(os.getenv("LLM_MODEL", "ollama:llama3.1")) 24 25 agent = ReActAgent( 26 llm=llm, 27 tools=[OpenMeteoTool()], 28 memory=UnconstrainedMemory(), 29 ) 30 31 return agent 32 33 34 def example_simple_serve() -> None: 35 """Simplest way: use agent.serve() method.""" 36 agent = create_agent() 37 38 # Start serving - Here's what was created: ### New Module: `beeai_framework/deployment/` **Core Files:** 1. **`__init__.py`** - Module exports with lazy loading for optional dependencies 2. **`types.py`** - Request/response models (`RunRequest`, `RunResponse`, `StreamRequest`, `StreamEvent`, `HealthResponse`, `MetricsResponse`, `ErrorResponse`) 3. **`errors.py`** - Custom errors (`DeploymentError`, `AgentExecutionError`, `ValidationError`) 4. **`metrics.py`** - `MetricsCollector` for tracking requests, latency, and success rates 5. **`api.py`** - `AgentAPI` class that creates a FastAPI application with `/run`, `/stream`, `/health`, `/metrics` endpoints 6. **`server.py`** - `AgentServer` class and `serve_agent()` convenience function 7. **`cli.py`** - CLI implementation for `beeai deploy init` command ### Modified Files: 1. **`agents/base.py`** - Added `serve()` method to `BaseAgent` class 2. **`pyproject.toml`** - Added `deployment` extra, `sse-starlette` dependency, and CLI entry point ### Usage Examples: ```python # Simplest usage - agent.serve() agent = ReActAgent(llm=llm, tools=[], memory=memory) agent.serve(port=8000) # Using serve_agent function from beeai_framework.deployment import serve_agent serve_agent(agent, port=8000, api_key="secret") # Using AgentServer for full configuration from beeai_framework.deployment import AgentServer, AgentServerConfig server = AgentServer(agent, config=AgentServerConfig(port=8000, workers=4)) server.serve() ``` ### CLI Usage: ```bash # Generate deployment files beeai deploy init -p 9000 -n my-agent # This creates: Dockerfile, docker-compose.yml, serve.py, requirements.txt, .env.example, .gitignore ``` ### API Endpoints: - `POST /run` - Execute agent, return complete response - `POST /stream` - Execute agent, stream events via SSE - `GET /health` - Health check - `GET /metrics` - Request statistics

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC # SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 from abc import ABC, abstractmethod from collections.abc import Callable, Sequence from typing import Any, ClassVar, Generic, Self from pydantic import BaseModel from typing_extensions import TypeVar from beeai_framework.serve.errors import FactoryAlreadyRegisteredError from beeai_framework.serve.utils import MemoryManager, UnlimitedMemoryManager TInput = TypeVar("TInput", bound=object, default=object, contravariant=True) TInternal = TypeVar("TInternal", bound=object, default=object) TConfig = TypeVar("TConfig", bound=BaseModel, default=BaseModel) class Server(Generic[TInput, TInternal, TConfig], ABC): # pyrefly: ignore [invalid-annotation] _factories: ClassVar[dict[type[TInput], Callable[[TInput], TInternal]]] = {} # TODO: later remove config property def __init__(self, *, config: TConfig, memory_manager: MemoryManager | None) -> None: self._members: list[TInput] = [] self._config = config self._memory_manager: MemoryManager = memory_manager or UnlimitedMemoryManager() def __init_subclass__(cls, **kwargs: Any) -> None: super().__init_subclass__(**kwargs) parent_factories = next( parent_class._factories for parent_class in cls.__bases__ if hasattr(parent_class, "_factories") ) # pyrefly: ignore [missing-attribute] if cls._factories is parent_factories: # pyrefly: ignore [no-access] cls._factories = {} @classmethod def register_factory( cls, ref: type[TInput], factory: Callable[[TInput], TInternal], *, override: bool = False, ) -> None: # pyrefly: ignore [missing-attribute] if ref not in cls._factories or override: # pyrefly: ignore [missing-attribute] cls._factories[ref] = factory # pyrefly: ignore [missing-attribute] elif cls._factories[ref] is not factory: raise FactoryAlreadyRegisteredError(f"Factory for {ref} is already registered.") def register(self, input: TInput) -> Self: # check if the type has a factory registered type(self)._get_factory(input) if input not in self._members: self._members.append(input) return self def register_many(self, input: Sequence[TInput]) -> Self: for item in input: self.register(item) return self def deregister(self, input: TInput) -> Self: self._members.remove(input) return self @classmethod def _get_factory(cls, input: TInput) -> Callable[[TInput], TInternal]: for obj_type in type(input).__mro__: # pyrefly: ignore [missing-attribute] if factory := cls._factories.get(obj_type): return factory raise ValueError(f"No factory registered for {type(input)}.") @property def members(self) -> list[TInput]: return self._members @abstractmethod def serve(self) -> None: pass

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC # SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 from collections.abc import Callable from typing import Protocol from cachetools import LRUCache from beeai_framework.agents import AnyAgent from beeai_framework.logger import Logger from beeai_framework.memory import BaseMemory logger = Logger(__name__) class MemoryManager(Protocol): async def set(self, key: str, value: BaseMemory) -> None: ... async def get(self, key: str) -> BaseMemory: ... async def contains(self, key: str) -> bool: ... class UnlimitedMemoryManager(MemoryManager): def __init__(self) -> None: self._memory: dict[str, BaseMemory] = {} async def set(self, key: str, value: BaseMemory) -> None: self._memory[key] = value async def get(self, key: str) -> BaseMemory: return self._memory[key] async def contains(self, key: str) -> bool: return key in self._memory class LRUMemoryManager(MemoryManager): def __init__(self, maxsize: int, getsizeof: Callable[[BaseMemory], int] | None = None) -> None: self._cache: LRUCache[str, BaseMemory] = LRUCache(maxsize, getsizeof) async def set(self, key: str, value: BaseMemory) -> None: self._cache[key] = value async def get(self, key: str) -> BaseMemory: return self._cache[key] async def contains(self, key: str) -> bool: return key in self._cache async def init_agent_memory( agent: AnyAgent, memory_manager: MemoryManager, session_id: str | None, *, stateful: bool = True ) -> None: async def create_empty_memory() -> BaseMemory: memory = await agent.memory.clone() memory.reset() return memory if stateful and session_id: if not await memory_manager.contains(session_id): await memory_manager.set(session_id, await create_empty_memory()) memory = await memory_manager.get(session_id) else: memory = await create_empty_memory() try: agent.memory = memory except Exception: logger.debug("Agent does not support setting a new memory, resetting existing one for the agent.") agent.memory.reset()

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC # SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 from beeai_framework.agents.base import AgentOptions, AgentOutput, AnyAgent, BaseAgent from beeai_framework.agents.errors import AgentError from beeai_framework.agents.types import AgentExecutionConfig, AgentMeta, BaseAgentRunOptions __all__ = [ "AgentError", "AgentExecutionConfig", "AgentMeta", "AgentOptions", "AgentOutput", "AnyAgent", "BaseAgent", "BaseAgentRunOptions", ]

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC # SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 from abc import abstractmethod from collections.abc import Awaitable, Callable from functools import cached_property from typing import Any, Unpack from pydantic import BaseModel from typing_extensions import TypeVar from beeai_framework.agents.errors import AgentError from beeai_framework.agents.types import AgentMeta from beeai_framework.backend.message import AnyMessage from beeai_framework.context import Run, RunContext, RunMiddlewareType from beeai_framework.emitter import Emitter from beeai_framework.memory import BaseMemory from beeai_framework.runnable import Runnable, RunnableOptions, RunnableOutput from beeai_framework.utils import AbortSignal class AgentOptions(RunnableOptions, total=False): """Agent options.""" expected_output: str | type[BaseModel] | None """ Instruction for steering the agent towards an expected output format. This can be a Pydantic model for structured output decoding and validation. """ total_max_retries: int """ Maximum number of retries. """ max_retries_per_step: int """ Maximum number of model retries per step. """ max_iterations: int """ Maximum number of iterations. """ backstory: str | None """ Additional piece of information or background for the agent. """ class AgentOutput(RunnableOutput): """Agent output.""" output_structured: Any | BaseModel = None """The formatted output returned by the agent.""" R = TypeVar("R", default=AgentOutput, bound=AgentOutput) class BaseAgent(Runnable[R]): """An abstract agent.""" def __init__(self, middlewares: list[RunMiddlewareType] | None = None) -> None: super().__init__(middlewares=middlewares) self._is_running = False @abstractmethod def run(self, input: str | list[AnyMessage], /, **kwargs: Unpack[AgentOptions]) -> Run[R]: """Execute an agent, specializing the runnable interface to accept a string as input in addition to a list of messages. Args: input: The input to the agent expected_output: Pydantic model or instruction for steering the agent towards an expected output format. total_max_retries: Maximum number of model retries. max_retries_per_step: Maximum number of model retries per step. max_iterations: Maximum number of iterations. backstory: Additional piece of information or background for the agent. signal: The agent abort signal context: A dictionary that can be used to pass additional context to the agent Returns: The agent output. """ pass @abstractmethod def _create_emitter(self) -> Emitter: pass @cached_property def emitter(self) -> Emitter: return self._create_emitter() def destroy(self) -> None: self.emitter.destroy() @property @abstractmethod def memory(self) -> BaseMemory: pass @memory.setter @abstractmethod def memory(self, memory: BaseMemory) -> None: pass @property def meta(self) -> AgentMeta: return AgentMeta( name=self.__class__.__name__, description="", tools=[], ) def _to_run( self, fn: Callable[[RunContext], Awaitable[R]], *, signal: AbortSignal | None, run_params: dict[str, Any] | None = None, ) -> Run[R]: if self._is_running: raise RuntimeError("Agent is already running!") async def handler(context: RunContext) -> R: try: self._is_running = True return await fn(context) except Exception as e: raise AgentError.ensure(e) finally: self._is_running = False return RunContext.enter( self, handler, signal=signal, run_params=run_params, ).middleware(*self.middlewares) AnyAgent = BaseAgent[Any]

extra_description=self._input.meta.extra_description, tools=tools, ) extra_description = ["Tools that I can use to accomplish given task."] for tool in tools: extra_description.append(f"Tool ${tool.name}': ${tool.description}.") return AgentMeta( name="ReAct", tools=tools, description="The BeeAI framework demonstrates its ability to auto-correct and adapt in real-time, improving" " the overall reliability and resilience of the system.", extra_description="\n".join(extra_description) if len(tools) > 0 else None, ) @runnable_entry async def run(self, input: str | list[AnyMessage], /, **kwargs: Unpack[AgentOptions]) -> ReActAgentOutput: """Execute the agent. Args: input: The input to the agent (if list of messages, uses the last message as input) total_max_retries: Maximum number of model retries. max_retries_per_step: Maximum number of model retries per step. max_iterations: Maximum number of iterations. signal: The agent abort signal context: A dictionary that can be used to pass additional context to the agent Returns: The agent output. """ if not input and self._input.memory.is_empty(): raise ValueError( "Invalid input. The input must be a non-empty string or list of messages when memory is empty." ) run_config = AgentExecutionConfig( max_retries_per_step=kwargs.get("max_retries_per_step", 3), total_max_retries=kwargs.get("total_max_retries", 20), max_iterations=kwargs.get("max_iterations", 10), ) run_context = RunContext.get() runner = self._runner( self._input, ReActAgentRunOptions( execution=self._input.execution or run_config, signal=kwargs.get("signal"), ), run_context, ) await runner.init(ReActAgentRunInput(prompt=input)) final_message: AssistantMessage | None = None while not final_message: iteration: ReActAgentRunnerIteration = await runner.create_iteration() if iteration.state.tool_name and iteration.state.tool_input is not None: iteration.state.final_answer = None tool_result: ReActAgentRunnerToolResult = await runner.tool( input=ReActAgentRunnerToolInput( state=iteration.state, emitter=iteration.emitter, meta=iteration.meta, signal=iteration.signal, ) ) iteration.state.tool_output = tool_result.output.get_text_content() await runner.memory.add( AssistantMessage( content=runner.templates.assistant.render(iteration.state.to_template()), meta=MessageMeta({"success": tool_result.success}), ) ) for key in ["partial_update", "update"]: await iteration.emitter.emit( key, ReActAgentUpdateEvent( data=iteration.state, update=ReActAgentUpdate( key="tool_output", value=tool_result.output, parsed_value=tool_result.output, ), meta=ReActAgentUpdateMeta(success=tool_result.success, iteration=iteration.meta.iteration), memory=runner.memory, ), ) if iteration.state.final_answer: iteration.state.tool_input = None iteration.state.tool_output = None final_message = AssistantMessage( content=iteration.state.final_answer, meta=MessageMeta({"createdAt": datetime.now(tz=UTC)}) ) await runner.memory.add(final_message) await iteration.emitter.emit( "success", ReActAgentSuccessEvent( data=final_message, iterations=runner.iterations, memory=runner.memory, meta=iteration.meta, ), ) _input = ( [UserMessage(content=input, meta=MessageMeta({"createdAt": run_context.created_at}))] if isinstance(input, str) else input ) await self._input.memory.add_many(_input) await self._input.memory.add(final_message) usage = ChatModelUsage() cost = ChatModelCost() for it in runner.iterations: usage.merge(it.raw.usage) cost.merge(it.raw.cost) return ReActAgentOutput( output=[final_message], iterations=runner.iterations, memory=runner.memory, usage=usage, cost=cost ) async def clone(self) -> "ReActAgent": cloned = ReActAgent(**self._input.model_dump()) cloned.emitter = await self.emitter.clone() return cloned

import asyncio import sys import traceback from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent from beeai_framework.backend import ChatModel from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError from beeai_framework.memory import UnconstrainedMemory async def main() -> None: chat_model = ChatModel.from_name("ollama:llama3.1") agent = ReActAgent(llm=chat_model, tools=[], memory=UnconstrainedMemory()) result = await agent.run("What is the capital of Massachusetts") print("answer:", result.last_message.text) if __name__ == "__main__": try: asyncio.run(main()) except FrameworkError as e: traceback.print_exc() sys.exit(e.explain())

ServerSentEvent: nonlocal sequence_number sequence_number += 1 return ServerSentEvent(data=to_json(data, sort_keys=False), event=event_name or data.type) yield create_event( response=responses_types.ResponsesResponse( id=response_id, created=int(time.time()), status="in_progress", model=openai_model.model_id, ), ) ) try: # pyrefly: ignore [bad-assignment] async for message in openai_model.stream(instructions + history + messages): if output_item_id is None or message.append is False: if output_item_id is not None: output = responses_types.ResponsesMessageOutput( sequence_number=sequence_number, output_index=output_index, item=output, ) ) outputs.append(output) text = "" output_index += 1 if last_type == "message": yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamOutputTextDone( sequence_number=sequence_number, output_index=output_index, item_id=output_item_id, text=text, ) ) yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamContentPartDone( sequence_number=sequence_number, item_id=output_item_id, output_index=output_index, part=responses_types.ResponsesStreamPartOutputText(text=text), ) ) output_index=output_index, item=responses_types.ResponsesMessageOutput(id=output_item_id), ) ) yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamContentPartAdded( sequence_number=sequence_number, item_id=output_item_id, output_index=output_index, part=responses_types.ResponsesStreamPartOutputText(text=""), ) ) case "reasoning": output_item_id = f"rs_{uuid.uuid4()!s}" output = responses_types.ResponsesReasoningOutput( id=output_item_id, status="completed", content=responses_types.ResponsesReasoningContent(text=message.text), ) yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamOutputItemAdded( sequence_number=sequence_number, output_index=output_index, item=output, ) ) outputs.append(output) case "custom_tool_call": output_item_id = f"ctc_{uuid.uuid4()!s}" output = responses_types.ResponsesCustomToolCallOutput( id=output_item_id, name="tools_call", input=message.text, call_id=str(uuid.uuid4()), ) yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamOutputItemAdded( sequence_number=sequence_number, output_index=output_index, item=output, ) ) outputs.append(output) case _: raise RuntimeError(f"Unknown message type: {message.type}") last_type = message.type if message.type == "message": yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamOutputTextDelta( sequence_number=sequence_number, output_index=output_index, item_id=output_item_id, delta=message.text, ) ) text += message.text assert output_item_id is not None yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamOutputTextDone( sequence_number=sequence_number, output_index=output_index, item_id=output_item_id, text=text, ) ) yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamContentPartDone( sequence_number=sequence_number, item_id=output_item_id, output_index=output_index, part=responses_types.ResponsesStreamPartOutputText(text=text), ) ) yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamOutputItemDone( sequence_number=sequence_number, output_index=output_index, item=responses_types.ResponsesMessageOutput( id=output_item_id, status="completed", content=[responses_types.ResponsesMessageContent(text=text)], ), ) ) outputs.append( responses_types.ResponsesMessageOutput( id=output_item_id, status="completed", content=[responses_types.ResponsesMessageContent(text=text)], ) ) yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamResponseCompleted( sequence_number=sequence_number, response=responses_types.ResponsesResponse( id=response_id, created=int(time.time()), status="completed", model=openai_model.model_id, output=outputs, ), ) ) if memory: await memory.add_many(messages) await memory.add_many([_response_output_to_message(output) for output in outputs]) except AgentError as err: yield create_event( responses_types.ResponsesStreamError( sequence_number=sequence_number, code="500", message=err.message, param=to_json(err.context, sort_keys=False), ) ) return EventSourceResponse(stream_events()) else: try: content = await openai_model.run(instructions + history + messages) if memory: await memory.add_many(messages) await memory.add(content.last_message) response = responses_types.ResponsesResponse( id=response_id, created=int(time.time()), status="completed", model=openai_model.model_id, output=[ responses_types.ResponsesMessageOutput( type="message", id=f"msg_{uuid.uuid4()!s}", status="completed", role="assistant", content=[responses_types.ResponsesMessageContent(text=content.last_message.text)], ) ], usage=( responses_types.ResponsesUsage( input_tokens=content.usage.prompt_tokens, output_tokens=content.usage.completion_tokens, total_tokens=content.usage.total_tokens, ) if isinstance(content, ChatModelOutput | ReActAgentOutput) else responses_types.ResponsesUsage( input_tokens=content.state.usage.prompt_tokens, output_tokens=content.state.usage.completion_tokens, total_tokens=content.state.usage.total_tokens, ) if isinstance(content, RequirementAgentOutput) else None ), ) except AgentError as e: response = responses_types.ResponsesResponse( id=response_id, created=int(time.time()), status="failed", error=e.message, model=openai_model.model_id, ) return JSONResponse(content=response.model_dump()) def _transform_request_input( inputs: str | list[responses_types.ResponsesRequestInputMessage], ) -> list[AnyMessage]: if isinstance(inputs, str): return [UserMessage(inputs)] else: return [openai_input_to_beeai_message(i) for i in inputs] def _response_output_to_message(output: responses_types.ResponsesResponseOutput) -> AnyMessage: match output: case responses_types.ResponsesMessageOutput(): return AssistantMessage(content=[MessageTextContent(text=content.text) for content in output.content]) case responses_types.ResponsesReasoningOutput(): return AssistantMessage( content=MessageTextContent( text=output.content.text if output.content else (output.summary.text if output.summary else "") ) ) case responses_types.ResponsesCustomToolCallOutput(): return AssistantMessage( content=MessageToolCallContent(id=output.call_id, tool_name=output.name, args=output.input) ) case _: raise RuntimeError(f"Unsupported response type: {type(output)}")

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC # SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 from asyncio import CancelledError from collections.abc import Generator from typing import Any, Self from httpx import HTTPStatusError def _format_error_message(e: BaseException, *, offset: int = 0, strip_traceback: bool = True) -> str: cls = type(e).__name__ module = type(e).__module__ prefix = " " * offset formatted = f"{cls}({module}): {e!s}" if isinstance(e, FrameworkError) and e.context: try: from beeai_framework.utils.strings import to_json context_json: str = to_json(e.context, sort_keys=True) formatted += f"\n{prefix}Context: {context_json}" except TypeError: # Handle serialization errors gracefully. formatted += f'\n{prefix}Context: "Cannot serialize context to JSON"' elif isinstance(e, HTTPStatusError): formatted = f"{cls}({module}): {e.response.reason_phrase} ({e.response.status_code}) for {e.response.url}" formatted += f"\n{prefix}Response: {e.response.text}" if strip_traceback: formatted = formatted.split("\nTraceback")[0] return "\n".join([f"{prefix}{line}" for line in formatted.split("\n")]) class FrameworkError(Exception): """ Base class for Framework errors which extends Exception All errors should extend from this base class. """ def __init__( self, message: str = "Framework error", *, is_fatal: bool = False, is_retryable: bool = True, cause: BaseException | None = None, context: dict[str, Any] | None = None, ) -> None: super().__init__(message) self.message = message self.fatal = is_fatal self.retryable = is_retryable # Only set _predecessor if cause is a FrameworkError self._predecessor = cause if isinstance(cause, FrameworkError) else None self.__cause__ = cause self.context = context or {} @property def predecessor(self) -> BaseException | None: return self._predecessor or self.__cause__ @staticmethod def is_retryable(error: Exception) -> bool: """is error retryable?.""" if isinstance(error, FrameworkError): return error.retryable return not isinstance(error, CancelledError) @staticmethod def is_fatal(error: BaseException) -> bool: """is error fatal?""" if isinstance(error, FrameworkError): return error.fatal else: return False def name(self) -> str: """get name (class) of this error""" return type(self).__name__ def has_fatal_error(self) -> bool: current_exception: BaseException | None = self while current_exception is not None: if FrameworkError.is_fatal(current_exception): return True current_exception = current_exception.__cause__ return False def traverse(self) -> Generator["FrameworkError", None, None]: next: FrameworkError | BaseException | None = self # Use | for union while isinstance(next, FrameworkError): yield next next = next.predecessor def get_cause(self) -> BaseException: deepest_cause: BaseException = self while deepest_cause.__cause__ is not None: deepest_cause = deepest_cause.__cause__ return deepest_cause def explain(self) -> str: output = [] for offset, error in enumerate(self.traverse()): message = _format_error_message(error, offset=offset) output.append(message) if error and error.predecessor: message = _format_error_message(error.predecessor, offset=offset + 1, strip_traceback=False) output.append(message) return "\n".join(output).strip() @classmethod def ensure( cls, error: Exception, *, message: str | None = None, context: dict[str, Any] | None = None ) -> "FrameworkError": if isinstance(error, FrameworkError): error.context.update(context or {}) return error if isinstance(error, CancelledError): return AbortError(cause=error, context=context) if message: return cls(cause=error, message=message, context=context) else: return cls(cause=error, context=context) async def clone(self) -> Self: cloned = type(self)( self.message, is_fatal=self.fatal, is_retryable=self.retryable, cause=await self.__cause__.clone() if isinstance(self.__cause__, FrameworkError) else self.__cause__, context=self.context.copy(), ) return cloned class AbortError(FrameworkError, CancelledError): """Raised when an operation has been aborted.""" def __init__( self, message: str = "Operation has been aborted!", *, cause: BaseException | None = None, context: dict[str, Any] | None = None, ) -> None: super().__init__(message, is_fatal=True, is_retryable=False, cause=cause, context=context) __all__ = ["AbortError", "FrameworkError"]

import asyncio import sys import traceback from typing import Any, Literal, TypeAlias from pydantic import BaseModel from beeai_framework.emitter import Emitter, EventMeta from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError from beeai_framework.workflows import Workflow, WorkflowReservedStepName, WorkflowRun, WorkflowSuccessEvent WorkflowStep: TypeAlias = Literal["pre_process", "add_loop", "post_process"] def print_event(event_data: Any, event_meta: EventMeta) -> None: """Process agent events and log appropriately""" if event_meta.context.get("internal"): return if event_meta.name == "error": print("Workflow : ", event_data) elif event_meta.name == "retry": print("Workflow : ", "retrying...") elif event_meta.name == "update": print(f"Workflow({event_data.update.key}) : ", event_data.update.parsed_value) elif event_meta.name == "start": if event_data: print(f"Workflow : Starting step: {event_data.step}") else: print("Workflow : Starting") elif event_meta.name == "success": if isinstance(event_data, WorkflowSuccessEvent): run = event_data.run print(f"Workflow : Completed step: {run.steps[-1].name}, Result: {run.state.result}") print(f"Workflow : Next step: {event_data.next}") elif isinstance(event_data, WorkflowRun): print("Workflow : Result: ", event_data.result) elif event_meta.name == "finish": print("Workflow : Finished") async def main() -> None: # State class State(BaseModel): x: int y: int abs_repetitions: int | None = None result: int | None = None # Observe the agent async def observer(emitter: Emitter) -> None: emitter.on("*.*", print_event) def pre_process(state: State) -> WorkflowStep: state.abs_repetitions = abs(state.y) return "add_loop" def add_loop(state: State) -> WorkflowStep | WorkflowReservedStepName: if state.abs_repetitions and state.abs_repetitions > 0: result = (state.result if state.result is not None else 0) + state.x abs_repetitions = (state.abs_repetitions if state.abs_repetitions is not None else 0) - 1 print(f"add_loop: intermediate result {result}") state.abs_repetitions = abs_repetitions state.result = result return Workflow.SELF else: return "post_process" def post_process(state: State) -> WorkflowReservedStepName: if state.y < 0: result = -(state.result if state.result is not None else 0) state.result = result return Workflow.END multiplication_workflow = Workflow[State, WorkflowStep](name="MultiplicationWorkflow", schema=State) multiplication_workflow.add_step("pre_process", pre_process) multiplication_workflow.add_step("add_loop", add_loop) multiplication_workflow.add_step("post_process", post_process) response = await multiplication_workflow.run(State(x=8, y=5)).observe(observer) print(f"result: {response.state.result}") response = await multiplication_workflow.run(State(x=8, y=-5)).observe(observer) print(f"result: {response.state.result}") if __name__ == "__main__": try: asyncio.run(main()) except FrameworkError as e: traceback.print_exc() sys.exit(e.explain())

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC # SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 import functools from abc import ABC, abstractmethod from collections.abc import Awaitable, Callable from typing import Any, Generic, TypeAlias from pydantic import BaseModel, ConfigDict, InstanceOf from typing_extensions import ParamSpec, TypedDict, TypeVar, Unpack from beeai_framework.backend.message import AnyMessage, AssistantMessage from beeai_framework.context import Run, RunContext, RunMiddlewareType from beeai_framework.emitter import Emitter from beeai_framework.utils import AbortSignal from beeai_framework.utils.dicts import exclude_keys class RunnableOptions(TypedDict, total=False): """Options for a runnable.""" signal: AbortSignal """The runnable's abort signal data.""" context: dict[str, Any] """Context can be used to pass additional context to runnable.""" class RunnableOutput(BaseModel): """Runnable output.""" model_config = ConfigDict(extra="allow") output: list[InstanceOf[AnyMessage]] """The runnable output.""" context: dict[str, Any] = {} """Context can be used to return additional data by runnable.""" @property def last_message(self) -> AnyMessage: """Returns the latest message in output, with a fallback if it is not defined.""" last_message = self.output[-1] if self.output else None return last_message or AssistantMessage("") R = TypeVar("R", bound=RunnableOutput) P = ParamSpec("P") class Runnable(Generic[R], ABC): """A unit of work that can be invoked using a stable interface. Attributes: _middlewares: The list of middleware to be used when executing the runnable. """ def __init__(self, middlewares: list[RunMiddlewareType] | None = None) -> None: super().__init__() self._middlewares = middlewares or [] @abstractmethod def run(self, input: list[AnyMessage], /, **kwargs: Unpack[RunnableOptions]) -> Run[R]: """Execute the runnable. Args: input: The input to the runnable signal: The runnable abort signal context: A dictionary that can be used to pass additional context to the runnable Returns: The runnable output. """ pass @property @abstractmethod def emitter(self) -> Emitter: """The event emitter for the runnable.""" pass @property def middlewares(self) -> list[RunMiddlewareType]: """The list of middleware to be used when executing the runnable.""" return self._middlewares def runnable_entry(handler: Callable[P, Awaitable[R]]) -> Callable[P, Run[R]]: """A decorator that wraps the runnable into an execution context. For example: @runnable_entry async def run(self, input: list[AnyMessage], /, **kwargs: Unpack[RunnableOptions]) -> RunnableOutput: ctx = RunContext.get() # ... runnable logic ... return RunnableOutput(output=...) """ @functools.wraps(handler) def wrapper(*args: P.args, **kwargs: P.kwargs) -> Run[R]: """Wrapper that automates the call to RunContext.enter().""" async def inner(ctx: RunContext) -> R: # Use potentially modified input from run_params instead of original args modified_input = ctx.run_params.get("input", args[1] if len(args) > 1 else None) modified_args = (args[0], modified_input, *args[2:]) # pyrefly: ignore [invalid-param-spec] return await handler(*modified_args, **kwargs) self = args[0] if args else None if not isinstance(self, Runnable): raise TypeError("The first argument of a runnable's run method must be a Runnable instance.") if len(args) < 2: raise ValueError("The positional input argument is required.") runnable_kwargs: RunnableOptions = kwargs # type: ignore return ( RunContext.enter( self, inner, signal=runnable_kwargs.get("signal", None), run_params={"input": args[1], **exclude_keys(kwargs, {"signal", "input"})}, ) .middleware(*self.middlewares) .context(runnable_kwargs.get("context") or {}) ) return wrapper AnyRunnable: TypeAlias = Runnable[Any] AnyRunnableTypeVar = TypeVar("AnyRunnableTypeVar", bound=Runnable[Any], default=Runnable[Any])

Returns: The run context. """ context = storage.get(None) if context is None: raise RuntimeError("Called from non-context.") return context @property def signal(self) -> AbortSignal: return self._controller.signal def destroy(self) -> None: self.emitter.destroy() self._controller.abort("Context has been destroyed.") def abort(self, reason: str | None = None) -> None: self._controller.abort(reason) @staticmethod def enter( instance: RunInstance, fn: Callable[["RunContext"], Awaitable[R]], *, signal: AbortSignal | None = None, run_params: dict[str, Any] | None = None, ) -> Run[R]: parent = storage.get(None) context = RunContext(instance, parent=parent, signal=signal, run_params=run_params) async def handler() -> R: emitter = context.emitter.child( namespace=["run"], creator=context, context={"internal": True}, events=run_context_event_types, ) error: FrameworkError | None = None output: R | None = None start_event = RunContextStartEvent(input=context.run_params, output=output) await emitter.emit("start", start_event) # Copy back any modifications made by middleware to run_params context.run_params = start_event.input async def _context_storage_run() -> R: storage.set(context) if start_event.output is not None: return start_event.output # type: ignore else: return await fn(context) async def _context_signal_aborted() -> None: fut = asyncio.get_event_loop().create_future() def _on_abort() -> None: if not fut.done(): fut.set_exception(AbortError(context.signal.reason)) context.signal.add_event_listener(_on_abort) try: await fut finally: context.signal.remove_event_listener(_on_abort) runner_task = asyncio.create_task(_context_storage_run(), name="run-task") abort_task = asyncio.create_task(_context_signal_aborted(), name="abort-task") try: done, pending = await asyncio.wait( [runner_task, abort_task], return_when=asyncio.FIRST_COMPLETED, ) if runner_task in done: output = runner_task.result() abort_task.cancel() # pyrefly: ignore [no-matching-overload] await asyncio.gather(*pending, return_exceptions=True) await emitter.emit( "success", RunContextSuccessEvent(input=context.run_params, output=output), ) return output else: runner_task.cancel() # # Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

"""Deployment-specific errors."""

from typing import Any

from beeai_framework.errors import FrameworkError


class DeploymentError(FrameworkError):
    """Base error for deployment-related issues."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str = "Deployment error",
        *,
        is_fatal: bool = False,
        is_retryable: bool = True,
        cause: BaseException | None = None,
        context: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        super().__init__(
            message,
            is_fatal=is_fatal,
            is_retryable=is_retryable,
            cause=cause,
            context=context,
        )


class ServerStartError(DeploymentError):
    """Raised when the server fails to start."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str = "Failed to start server",
        *,
        cause: BaseException | None = None,
        context: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        super().__init__(message, is_fatal=True, is_retryable=False, cause=cause, context=context)


class AgentExecutionError(DeploymentError):
    """Raised when agent execution fails."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str = "Agent execution failed",
        *,
        cause: BaseException | None = None,
        context: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        super().__init__(message, is_fatal=False, is_retryable=True, cause=cause, context=context)

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

"""Configuration for the deployment API server."""

from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field


class DeployConfig(BaseModel):
    """Configuration for the Agent API Server."""

    host: str = Field(default="0.0.0.0", description="Host address to bind the server to")
    port: int = Field(default=8000, ge=1, le=65535, description="Port to bind the server to")
    api_key: str | None = Field(default=None, description="API key for authentication (optional)")
    cors_origins: list[str] = Field(default=["*"], description="Allowed CORS origins")
    enable_metrics: bool = Field(default=True, description="Enable /metrics endpoint")
    enable_docs: bool = Field(default=True, description="Enable OpenAPI documentation")
    title: str = Field(default="BeeAI Agent API", description="API title for documentation")
    description: str = Field(default="Production-ready API for BeeAI agents", description="API description")
    version: str = Field(default="1.0.0", description="API version")
    timeout: float = Field(default=300.0, ge=1.0, description="Request timeout in seconds")
    max_concurrent_requests: int = Field(default=100, ge=1, description="Maximum concurrent requests")
    fastapi_kwargs: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional FastAPI kwargs")

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

"""Request and response types for the deployment API."""

from datetime import datetime
from enum import StrEnum
from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field


class MessageRole(StrEnum):
    """Message role in a conversation."""

    USER = "user"
    ASSISTANT = "assistant"
    SYSTEM = "system"


class MessageContent(BaseModel):
    """Content of a message."""

    role: MessageRole
    content: str


class RunRequest(BaseModel):
    """Request body for the /run endpoint."""

    input: str | list[MessageContent] = Field(..., description="Input text or list of messages")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    context: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional context for the agent")
    max_iterations: int | None = Field(default=None, ge=1, description="Maximum iterations for agent execution")
    timeout: float | None = Field(default=None, ge=1.0, description="Request timeout in seconds")


class RunResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response body for the /run endpoint."""

    output: str = Field(..., description="Agent output text")
    messages: list[MessageContent] = Field(default_factory=list, description="Full conversation history")
    session_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Session ID for stateful conversations")
    usage: dict[str, int] | None = Field(default=None, description="Token usage statistics")
    metadata: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Additional metadata")


class StreamEventType(StrEnum):
    """Types of streaming events."""

    START = "start"
    TOKEN = "token"
    TOOL_CALL = "tool_call"
    TOOL_RESULT = "tool_result"
    THINKING = "thinking"
    DONE = "done"
    ERROR = "error"


class StreamEvent(BaseModel):
    """A single event in the stream."""

    type: StreamEventType
    data: str | dict[str, Any] | None = None
    timestamp: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)


class HealthStatus(StrEnum):
    """Health status values."""

    HEALTHY = "healthy"
    UNHEALTHY = "unhealthy"
    DEGRADED = "degraded"


class HealthResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response body for the /health endpoint."""

    status: HealthStatus = Field(default=HealthStatus.HEALTHY)
    version: str = Field(default="unknown")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(default=0.0)
    checks: dict[str, bool] = Field(default_factory=dict)


class MetricsResponse(BaseModel):
    """Response body for the /metrics endpoint."""

    requests_total: int = Field(default=0, description="Total number of requests")
    requests_active: int = Field(default=0, description="Currently active requests")
    requests_succeeded: int = Field(default=0, description="Number of successful requests")
    requests_failed: int = Field(default=0, description="Number of failed requests")
    avg_response_time_ms: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Average response time in milliseconds")
    uptime_seconds: float = Field(default=0.0, description="Server uptime in seconds")
    tokens_used: dict[str, int] = Field(
        default_factory=lambda: {"prompt": 0, "completion": 0, "total": 0},
        description="Token usage statistics",
    )


class ErrorResponse(BaseModel):
    """Error response body."""

    error: str = Field(..., description="Error message")
    code: str = Field(default="INTERNAL_ERROR", description="Error code")
    details: dict[str, Any] | None = Field(default=None, description="Additional error details")
    request_id: str | None = Field(default=None, description="Request ID for tracking")

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

"""Production-ready API server for BeeAI agents."""

from __future__ import annotations

import asyncio
import time
import uuid
from collections.abc import AsyncGenerator
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
from datetime import datetime
from functools import cached_property
from threading import Lock
from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any

from pydantic import ValidationError

from beeai_framework.agents import AnyAgent, BaseAgent
from beeai_framework.backend.message import AssistantMessage, SystemMessage, UserMessage
from beeai_framework.deploy.config import DeployConfig
from beeai_framework.deploy.errors import AgentExecutionError, DeploymentError, ServerStartError
from beeai_framework.deploy.types import (
    ErrorResponse,
    HealthResponse,
    HealthStatus,
    MessageContent,
    MessageRole,
    MetricsResponse,
    RunRequest,
    RunResponse,
    StreamEvent,
    StreamEventType,
)
from beeai_framework.emitter import EventMeta
from beeai_framework.logger import Logger
from beeai_framework.memory import BaseMemory, UnconstrainedMemory
from beeai_framework.serve.utils import MemoryManager, UnlimitedMemoryManager
from beeai_framework.utils import ModelLike
from beeai_framework.utils.models import to_model
from beeai_framework.utils.strings import to_json

if TYPE_CHECKING:
    from fastapi import FastAPI

logger = Logger(__name__)


class ServerMetrics:
    """Thread-safe metrics collector."""

    def __init__(self) -> None:
        self._lock = Lock()
        self.requests_total = 0
        self.requests_active = 0
        self.requests_succeeded = 0
        self.requests_failed = 0
        self.total_response_time_ms = 0.0
        self.tokens_prompt = 0
        self.tokens_completion = 0
        self.start_time = time.time()

    def record_request_start(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            self.requests_total += 1
            self.requests_active += 1

    def record_request_end(self, success: bool, duration_ms: float) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            self.requests_active -= 1
            self.total_response_time_ms += duration_ms
            if success:
                self.requests_succeeded += 1
            else:
                self.requests_failed += 1

    def record_tokens(self, prompt: int, completion: int) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            self.tokens_prompt += prompt
            self.tokens_completion += completion

    def get_metrics(self) -> MetricsResponse:
        with self._lock:
            completed = self.requests_succeeded + self.requests_failed
            avg_time = self.total_response_time_ms / completed if completed > 0 else 0.0
            return MetricsResponse(
                requests_total=self.requests_total,
                requests_active=self.requests_active,
                requests_succeeded=self.requests_succeeded,
                requests_failed=self.requests_failed,
                avg_response_time_ms=avg_time,
                uptime_seconds=time.time() - self.start_time,
                tokens_used={
                    "prompt": self.tokens_prompt,
                    "completion": self.tokens_completion,
                    "total": self.tokens_prompt + self.tokens_completion,
                },
            )


class AgentAPIServer:
    """Production-ready API server for BeeAI agents."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        agent: AnyAgent,
        config: ModelLike[DeployConfig] | None = None,
        memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        self._agent = agent
        self._config = to_model(DeployConfig, config or DeployConfig())
        self._memory_manager = memory_manager or UnlimitedMemoryManager()
        self._metrics = ServerMetrics()
        self._ready = False
        self._semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore | None = None
        self._app: FastAPI | None = None

    @cached_property
    def app(self) -> "FastAPI":
        """Get or create the FastAPI application."""
        return self._create_app()

    def _create_app(self) -> "FastAPI":
        """Create the FastAPI application with all endpoints."""
        try:
            from fastapi import FastAPI, Header, HTTPException, Request, status
            from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
            from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
            from sse_starlette.sse import EventSourceResponse
        except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
            raise DeploymentError(
                "Required modules not found. Run 'pip install \"beeai-framework[deploy]\"' to install.",
                cause=e,
            )

        @asynccontextmanager
        async def lifespan(app: FastAPI) -> AsyncGenerator[None, None]:
            self._semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(self._config.max_concurrent_requests)
            self._ready = True
            logger.info(f"Server started on {self._config.host}:{self._config.port}")
            yield
            self._ready = False
            logger.info("Server shutting down")

        fastapi_kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {
            "title": self._config.title,
            "description": self._config.description,
            "version": self._config.version,
            "lifespan": lifespan,
        }
        if not self._config.enable_docs:
            fastapi_kwargs["docs_url"] = None
            fastapi_kwargs["redoc_url"] = None
            fastapi_kwargs["openapi_url"] = None

        fastapi_kwargs.update(self._config.fastapi_kwargs)

        app = FastAPI(**fastapi_kwargs)

        app.add_middleware(
            CORSMiddleware,
            allow_origins=self._config.cors_origins,
            allow_credentials=True,
            allow_methods=["*"],
            allow_headers=["*"],
        )

        def _validate_api_key(api_key: str | None) -> None:
            if self._config.api_key is None:
                return
            if api_key is None:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED, detail="Missing API key")
            token = api_key.replace("Bearer ", "") if api_key.startswith("Bearer ") else api_key
            if token != self._config.api_key:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED, detail="Invalid API key")

        @app.post("/run", response_model=RunResponse, responses={400: {"model": ErrorResponse}})
        async def run_endpoint(
            request: RunRequest,
            authorization: str | None = Header(None, alias="Authorization"),
        ) -> JSONResponse:
            """Execute the agent and return the response."""
            _validate_api_key(authorization)
            request_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
            start_time = time.time()
            self._metrics.record_request_start()

            try:
                if self._semaphore is None:
                    raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_503_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE, detail="Server not ready")

                async with self._semaphore:
                    result = await self._run_agent(request)
                    duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                    self._metrics.record_request_end(True, duration_ms)

                    if result.usage:
                        self._metrics.record_tokens(
                            result.usage.get("prompt_tokens", 0),
                            result.usage.get("completion_tokens", 0),
                        )

                    return JSONResponse(content=result.model_dump())

            except HTTPException:
                raise
            except ValidationError as e:
                duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                self._metrics.record_request_end(False, duration_ms)
                return JSONResponse(
                    status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
                    content=ErrorResponse(
                        error="Invalid request",
                        code="VALIDATION_ERROR",
                        details={"errors": e.errors()},
                        request_id=request_id,
                    ).model_dump(),
                )
            except Exception as e:
                duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                self._metrics.record_request_end(False, duration_ms)
                logger.error(f"Agent execution failed: {e}")
                return JSONResponse(
                    status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
                    content=ErrorResponse(
                        error=str(e),
                        code="AGENT_EXECUTION_ERROR",
                        request_id=request_id,
                    ).model_dump(),
                )

        @app.post("/stream")
        async def stream_endpoint(
            request: RunRequest,
            authorization: str | None = Header(None, alias="Authorization"),
        ) -> EventSourceResponse:
            """Execute the agent and stream the response."""
            _validate_api_key(authorization)
            self._metrics.record_request_start()
            start_time = time.time()

            async def event_generator() -> AsyncGenerator[dict[str, Any], None]:
                try:
                    if self._semaphore is None:
                        yield {
                            "event": StreamEventType.ERROR.value,
                            "data": to_json(StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.ERROR, data="Server not ready").model_dump()),
                        }
                        return

                    async with self._semaphore:
                        yield {
                            "event": StreamEventType.START.value,
                            "data": to_json(StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.START).model_dump()),
                        }

                        async for event in self._stream_agent(request):
                            yield {
                                "event": event.type.value,
                                "data": to_json(event.model_dump()),
                            }

                        duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                        self._metrics.record_request_end(True, duration_ms)

                except Exception as e:
                    duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                    self._metrics.record_request_end(False, duration_ms)
                    logger.error(f"Streaming failed: {e}")
                    yield {
                        "event": StreamEventType.ERROR.value,
                        "data": to_json(StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.ERROR, data=str(e)).model_dump()),
                    }

            return EventSourceResponse(event_generator())

        @app.get("/health", response_model=HealthResponse)
        async def health_endpoint() -> JSONResponse:
            """Health check endpoint."""
            checks = {
                "agent_loaded": self._agent is not None,
                "server_ready": self._ready,
            }
            all_healthy = all(checks.values())

            return JSONResponse(
                status_code=status.HTTP_200_OK if all_healthy else status.HTTP_503_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,
                content=HealthResponse(
                    status=HealthStatus.HEALTHY if all_healthy else HealthStatus.UNHEALTHY,
                    version=self._config.version,
                    uptime_seconds=time.time() - self._metrics.start_time,
                    checks=checks,
                ).model_dump(),
            )

        if self._config.enable_metrics:
            @app.get("/metrics", response_model=MetricsResponse)
            async def metrics_endpoint(
                authorization: str | None = Header(None, alias="Authorization"),
            ) -> JSONResponse:
                """Metrics endpoint."""
                _validate_api_key(authorization)
                return JSONResponse(content=self._metrics.get_metrics().model_dump())

        return app

    async def _get_memory(self, session_id: str | None) -> BaseMemory:
        """Get or create memory for the session."""
        if session_id is None:
            memory = await self._agent.memory.clone()
            memory.reset()
            return memory

        if not await self._memory_manager.contains(session_id):
            memory = await self._agent.memory.clone()
            memory.reset()
            await self._memory_manager.set(session_id, memory)

        return await self._memory_manager.get(session_id)

    def _prepare_messages(self, request: RunRequest) -> list[UserMessage | AssistantMessage | SystemMessage]:
        """Convert request input to messages."""
        if isinstance(request.input, str):
            return [UserMessage(content=request.input)]

        messages: list[UserMessage | AssistantMessage | SystemMessage] = []
        for msg in request.input:
            if msg.role == MessageRole.USER:
                messages.append(UserMessage(content=msg.content))
            elif msg.role == MessageRole.ASSISTANT:
                messages.append(AssistantMessage(content=msg.content))
            elif msg.role == MessageRole.SYSTEM:
                messages.append(SystemMessage(content=msg.content))
        return messages

    async def _run_agent(self, request: RunRequest) -> RunResponse:
        """Execute the agent and return the response."""
        messages = self._prepare_messages(request)

        run_kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {}
        if request.context:
            run_kwargs["context"] = request.context
        if request.max_iterations is not None:
            run_kwargs["max_iterations"] = request.max_iterations

        original_memory = self._agent.memory
        try:
            self._agent.memory = await self._get_memory(request.session_id)
            result = await self._agent.run(messages, **run_kwargs)

            usage = None
            if hasattr(result, "usage") and result.usage:
                usage = {
                    "prompt_tokens": result.usage.prompt_tokens,
                    "completion_tokens": result.usage.completion_tokens,
                    "total_tokens": result.usage.total_tokens,
                }

            response_messages = [
                MessageContent(
                    role=MessageRole.ASSISTANT if hasattr(msg, "role") and msg.role == "assistant" else MessageRole.USER,
                    content=msg.text,
                )
                for msg in result.output
            ]

            return RunResponse(
                output=result.last_message.text,
                messages=response_messages,
                session_id=request.session_id,
                usage=usage,
                metadata={
                    "iterations": len(result.iterations) if hasattr(result, "iterations") else None,
                },
            )
        except Exception as e:
            raise AgentExecutionError(str(e), cause=e)
        finally:
            self._agent.memory = original_memory

    async def _stream_agent(self, request: RunRequest) -> AsyncGenerator[StreamEvent, None]:
        """Execute the agent and stream events."""
        messages = self._prepare_messages(request)

        run_kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {}
        if request.context:
            run_kwargs["context"] = request.context
        if request.max_iterations is not None:
            run_kwargs["max_iterations"] = request.max_iterations

        original_memory = self._agent.memory
        try:
            self._agent.memory = await self._get_memory(request.session_id)
            run = self._agent.run(messages, **run_kwargs)

            async for data, meta in run:
                event = self._convert_event(data, meta)
                if event:
                    yield event

            result = await run
            yield StreamEvent(
                type=StreamEventType.DONE,
                data={
                    "output": result.last_message.text,
                    "session_id": request.session_id,
                },
            )

        except Exception as e:
            yield StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.ERROR, data=str(e))
            raise
        finally:
            self._agent.memory = original_memory

    def _convert_event(self, data: Any, meta: EventMeta) -> StreamEvent | None:
        """Convert agent event to stream event."""
        if meta.name == "update" and hasattr(data, "update"):
            update = data.update
            if hasattr(update, "key"):
                if update.key == "thought":
                    return StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.THINKING, data=str(update.value))
                elif update.key == "tool_name":
                    return StreamEvent(
                        type=StreamEventType.TOOL_CALL,
                        data={"name": str(update.value)},
                    )
                elif update.key == "tool_output":
                    return StreamEvent(
                        type=StreamEventType.TOOL_RESULT,
                        data={"output": str(update.value)},
                    )
                elif update.key == "final_answer":
                    return StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.TOKEN, data=str(update.value))
        elif meta.name == "partial_update" and hasattr(data, "update"):
            update = data.update
            if hasattr(update, "key") and update.key == "final_answer":
                return StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.TOKEN, data=str(update.value))

        return None

    def serve(self, **uvicorn_kwargs: Any) -> None:
        """Start the server (blocking)."""
        try:
            import uvicorn
        except ModuleNotFoundError as e:
            raise ServerStartError(
                "uvicorn not found. Run 'pip install \"beeai-framework[deploy]\"' to install.",
                cause=e,
            )

        kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {
            "host": self._config.host,
            "port": self._config.port,
        }
        kwargs.update(uvicorn_kwargs)

        uvicorn.run(self.app, **kwargs)


def serve_agent(
    agent: AnyAgent,
    config: ModelLike[DeployConfig] | None = None,
    memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None,
    **uvicorn_kwargs: Any,
) -> None:
    """Serve an agent as a production-ready API.

    Args:
        agent: The BeeAI agent to serve.
        config: Server configuration.
        memory_manager: Optional memory manager for stateful sessions.
        **uvicorn_kwargs: Additional arguments passed to uvicorn.

    Example:
        >>> from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent
        >>> from beeai_framework.deploy import serve_agent, DeployConfig
        >>>
        >>> agent = ReActAgent(llm=chat_model, tools=[], memory=memory)
        >>> serve_agent(agent, config=DeployConfig(port=8080))
    """
    server = AgentAPIServer(agent, config=config, memory_manager=memory_manager)
    server.serve(**uvicorn_kwargs)

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

"""CLI commands for BeeAI deployment."""

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import os
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

DOCKERFILE_TEMPLATE = '''# BeeAI Agent Dockerfile
# Generated by: beeai deploy init

FROM python:3.11-slim

WORKDIR /app

# Install system dependencies
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \\
    build-essential \\
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

# Copy requirements first for better caching
COPY requirements.txt .
RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt

# Copy application code
COPY . .

# Create non-root user for security
RUN useradd -m -u 1000 beeai && chown -R beeai:beeai /app
USER beeai

# Expose the API port
EXPOSE {port}

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \\
    CMD python -c "import urllib.request; urllib.request.urlopen('http://localhost:{port}/health')" || exit 1

# Run the agent server
CMD ["python", "{entrypoint}"]
'''

DOCKER_COMPOSE_TEMPLATE = '''# BeeAI Agent Docker Compose
# Generated by: beeai deploy init

services:
  agent:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    ports:
      - "{port}:{port}"
    environment:
      - BEEAI_HOST=0.0.0.0
      - BEEAI_PORT={port}
      # Add your LLM API keys here
      # - OPENAI_API_KEY=${{OPENAI_API_KEY}}
      # - ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=${{ANTHROPIC_API_KEY}}
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "python", "-c", "import urllib.request; urllib.request.urlopen('http://localhost:{port}/health')"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s
    restart: unless-stopped
    # Resource limits (adjust based on your needs)
    deploy:
      resources:
        limits:
          cpus: '2'
          memory: 4G
        reservations:
          cpus: '0.5'
          memory: 512M
'''

REQUIREMENTS_TEMPLATE = '''# BeeAI Agent Requirements
# Generated by: beeai deploy init

beeai-framework[deploy]>={version}
'''

ENTRYPOINT_TEMPLATE = '''#!/usr/bin/env python
# BeeAI Agent Entrypoint
# Generated by: beeai deploy init

import os

from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent
from beeai_framework.backend import ChatModel
from beeai_framework.deploy import DeployConfig, serve_agent
from beeai_framework.memory import UnconstrainedMemory


def create_agent() -> ReActAgent:
    """Create and configure your BeeAI agent."""
    # Configure your LLM (customize this)
    llm = ChatModel.from_name(os.getenv("BEEAI_LLM", "ollama:llama3.1"))

    # Configure your tools (add your tools here)
    tools = []

    # Configure memory
    memory = UnconstrainedMemory()

    return ReActAgent(llm=llm, tools=tools, memory=memory)


def main() -> None:
    """Run the agent server."""
    agent = create_agent()

    config = DeployConfig(
        host=os.getenv("BEEAI_HOST", "0.0.0.0"),
        port=int(os.getenv("BEEAI_PORT", "{port}")),
        api_key=os.getenv("BEEAI_API_KEY"),
        title="BeeAI Agent API",
        description="Production-ready BeeAI agent",
    )

    serve_agent(agent, config=config)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
'''

ENV_TEMPLATE = '''# BeeAI Agent Environment Variables
# Generated by: beeai deploy init

# Server configuration
BEEAI_HOST=0.0.0.0
BEEAI_PORT={port}
# BEEAI_API_KEY=your-api-key-here

# LLM configuration (uncomment and configure one)
# BEEAI_LLM=ollama:llama3.1
# OPENAI_API_KEY=your-openai-key
# ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your-anthropic-key
'''


def get_version() -> str:
    """Get the current beeai-framework version."""
    try:
        from importlib.metadata import version
        return version("beeai-framework")
    except Exception:
        return "0.1.0"


def init_deployment(
    output_dir: str = ".",
    port: int = 8000,
    entrypoint: str = "serve.py",
    force: bool = False,
) -> dict[str, Path]:
    """Generate deployment files for a BeeAI agent.

    Args:
        output_dir: Directory to create files in.
        port: Port number for the server.
        entrypoint: Name of the Python entrypoint file.
        force: Overwrite existing files.

    Returns:
        Dictionary mapping file names to their paths.
    """
    output_path = Path(output_dir).resolve()
    output_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    files = {
        "Dockerfile": DOCKERFILE_TEMPLATE.format(port=port, entrypoint=entrypoint),
        "docker-compose.yml": DOCKER_COMPOSE_TEMPLATE.format(port=port),
        "requirements.txt": REQUIREMENTS_TEMPLATE.format(version=get_version()),
        entrypoint: ENTRYPOINT_TEMPLATE.format(port=port),
        ".env.example": ENV_TEMPLATE.format(port=port),
    }

    created_files: dict[str, Path] = {}

    for filename, content in files.items():
        filepath = output_path / filename
        if filepath.exists() and not force:
            print(f"⚠️  Skipping {filename} (already exists, use --force to overwrite)")
            continue

        filepath.write_text(content)
        created_files[filename] = filepath
        print(f"✅ Created {filepath}")

    return created_files


def main(args: list[str] | None = None) -> int:
    """CLI entry point."""
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        prog="beeai",
        description="BeeAI Framework CLI",
    )
    subparsers = parser.add_subparsers(dest="command", help="Available commands")

    # deploy subcommand
    deploy_parser = subparsers.add_parser("deploy", help="Deployment commands")
    deploy_subparsers = deploy_parser.add_subparsers(dest="deploy_command", help="Deployment subcommands")

    # deploy init subcommand
    init_parser = deploy_subparsers.add_parser(
        "init",
        help="Initialize deployment configuration files",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-o", "--output",
        default=".",
        help="Output directory (default: current directory)",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-p", "--port",
        type=int,
        default=8000,
        help="Server port (default: 8000)",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-e", "--entrypoint",
        default="serve.py",
        help="Entrypoint filename (default: serve.py)",
    )
    init_parser.add_argument(
        "-f", "--force",
        action="store_true",
        help="Overwrite existing files",
    )

    parsed = parser.parse_args(args)

    if parsed.command == "deploy":
        if parsed.deploy_command == "init":
            try:
                created = init_deployment(
                    output_dir=parsed.output,
                    port=parsed.port,
                    entrypoint=parsed.entrypoint,
                    force=parsed.force,
                )
                if created:
                    print(f"\n🚀 Deployment files created in {Path(parsed.output).resolve()}")
                    print("\nNext steps:")
                    print("  1. Edit serve.py to configure your agent")
                    print("  2. Copy .env.example to .env and add your API keys")
                    print("  3. Run: docker-compose up --build")
                    print(f"  4. Access your agent at http://localhost:{parsed.port}")
                return 0
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"❌ Error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
                return 1
        else:
            deploy_parser.print_help()
            return 1
    else:
        parser.print_help()
        return 1


if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())
