    def serve(
        self,
        config: ModelLike[DeployConfig] | None = None,
        memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None,
        **uvicorn_kwargs: Any,
    ) -> None:
        """Serve the agent as a production-ready API.

        This method starts an HTTP server that exposes the agent through REST endpoints:
        - POST /run: Execute the agent and return the response
        - POST /stream: Execute the agent and stream the response
        - GET /health: Health check endpoint
        - GET /metrics: Server metrics (if enabled)

        Args:
            config: Server configuration (host, port, API key, etc.)
            memory_manager: Optional memory manager for stateful sessions.
            **uvicorn_kwargs: Additional arguments passed to uvicorn.

        Example:
            >>> from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent
            >>> from beeai_framework.deploy import DeployConfig
            >>>
            >>> agent = ReActAgent(llm=chat_model, tools=[], memory=memory)
            >>> agent.serve(config=DeployConfig(port=8080))
        """
        from beeai_framework.deploy.api import AgentAPIServer

        server = AgentAPIServer(self, config=config, memory_manager=memory_manager)
        server.serve(**uvicorn_kwargs)

    def create_server(
        self,
        config: ModelLike[DeployConfig] | None = None,
        memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None,
    ) -> AgentAPIServer:
        """Create an API server for the agent without starting it.

        This allows for more control over the server lifecycle, such as
        integrating with existing ASGI applications or testing.

        Args:
            config: Server configuration.
            memory_manager: Optional memory manager for stateful sessions.

        Returns:
            An AgentAPIServer instance with the FastAPI app available as server.app.

        Example:
            >>> server = agent.create_server(config=DeployConfig(port=8080))
            >>> # Access the FastAPI app for integration
            >>> app = server.app
        """
        from beeai_framework.deploy.api import AgentAPIServer

        return AgentAPIServer(self, config=config, memory_manager=memory_manager)

import requests

from beeai_framework.backend.message import AnyMessage, AssistantMessage
from beeai_framework.deploy.api import AgentAPIServer
from beeai_framework.deploy.config import DeployConfig
from beeai_framework.emitter import Emitter
from beeai_framework.memory import BaseMemory, UnconstrainedMemory
from beeai_framework.runnable import Runnable, RunnableOptions, RunnableOutput, runnable_entry
from beeai_framework.serve.utils import UnlimitedMemoryManager

TEST_API_KEY = "test-api-key-12345"


class MockAgent(Runnable[RunnableOutput]):
    """Mock agent for testing."""

    def __init__(self) -> None:
        super().__init__()
        self._memory = UnconstrainedMemory()

    @property
    def emitter(self) -> Emitter:
        return Emitter.root().child(namespace=["mock", "agent"])

    @property
    def memory(self) -> BaseMemory:
        return self._memory

    @memory.setter
    def memory(self, memory: BaseMemory) -> None:
        self._memory = memory

    @runnable_entry
    async def run(self, input: list[AnyMessage], /, **kwargs: Unpack[RunnableOptions]) -> RunnableOutput:
        last_input = input[-1].text if input else "empty"
        return RunnableOutput(output=[AssistantMessage(content=f"Echo: {last_input}")])


@pytest.fixture(scope="module")
def test_server() -> Generator[str, None, None]:
    """Start a test server for the mock agent."""
    port = 19101

    config = DeployConfig(
        host="127.0.0.1",
        port=port,
        api_key=TEST_API_KEY,
        enable_docs=True,
        enable_metrics=True,
    )

    agent = MockAgent()
    server = AgentAPIServer(agent, config=config)

    thread = threading.Thread(target=server.serve, daemon=True)
    thread.start()

    server_url = f"http://127.0.0.1:{port}"

    for _ in range(30):
        try:
            resp = requests.get(f"{server_url}/health", timeout=0.2)
            if resp.status_code == 200:
                break
        except requests.exceptions.ConnectionError:
            time.sleep(0.1)
    else:
        pytest.fail(f"Server did not become reachable at {server_url}")

    yield server_url

    with contextlib.suppress(Exception):
        pass


@pytest.fixture(scope="module")
def test_server_no_auth() -> Generator[str, None, None]:
    """Start a test server without API key authentication."""
    port = 19102

    config = DeployConfig(
        host="127.0.0.1",
        port=port,
        api_key=None,
        enable_docs=False,
        enable_metrics=True,
    )

    agent = MockAgent()
    server = AgentAPIServer(agent, config=config)

    thread = threading.Thread(target=server.serve, daemon=True)
    thread.start()

    server_url = f"http://127.0.0.1:{port}"

    for _ in range(30):
        try:
            resp = requests.get(f"{server_url}/health", timeout=0.2)
            if resp.status_code == 200:
                break
        except requests.exceptions.ConnectionError:
            time.sleep(0.1)
    else:
        pytest.fail(f"Server did not become reachable at {server_url}")

    yield server_url


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_run_endpoint_success(test_server: str) -> None:
    """Test successful /run endpoint."""
    url = f"{test_server}/run"

    payload = {"input": "Hello, World!"}
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {TEST_API_KEY}"}

    response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=10)

    assert response.status_code == 200
    data = response.json()
    assert "output" in data
    assert "Echo: Hello, World!" in data["output"]


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_run_endpoint_with_messages(test_server: str) -> None:
    """Test /run endpoint with message list."""
    url = f"{test_server}/run"

    payload = {
        "input": [
            {"role": "user", "content": "First message"},
            {"role": "user", "content": "Second message"},
        ]
    }
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {TEST_API_KEY}"}

    response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=10)

    assert response.status_code == 200
    data = response.json()
    assert "output" in data
    assert "Echo: Second message" in data["output"]


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_run_endpoint_auth_required(test_server: str) -> None:
    """Test /run endpoint requires authentication."""
    url = f"{test_server}/run"

    payload = {"input": "Hello"}

    response = requests.post(url, json=payload, timeout=10)
    assert response.status_code == 401


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_run_endpoint_invalid_api_key(test_server: str) -> None:
    """Test /run endpoint rejects invalid API key."""
    url = f"{test_server}/run"

    payload = {"input": "Hello"}
    headers = {"Authorization": "Bearer wrong-key"}

    response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=10)
    assert response.status_code == 401


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_health_endpoint(test_server: str) -> None:
    """Test /health endpoint."""
    url = f"{test_server}/health"

    response = requests.get(url, timeout=10)

    assert response.status_code == 200
    data = response.json()
    assert data["status"] == "healthy"
    assert "uptime_seconds" in data
    assert "checks" in data
    assert data["checks"]["agent_loaded"] is True
    assert data["checks"]["server_ready"] is True


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_metrics_endpoint(test_server: str) -> None:
    """Test /metrics endpoint."""
    url = f"{test_server}/metrics"
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {TEST_API_KEY}"}

    response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=10)

    assert response.status_code == 200
    data = response.json()
    assert "requests_total" in data
    assert "requests_active" in data
    assert "requests_succeeded" in data
    assert "requests_failed" in data
    assert "avg_response_time_ms" in data
    assert "uptime_seconds" in data
    assert "tokens_used" in data

    assert response.status_code == 401


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_server_without_auth(test_server_no_auth: str) -> None:
    """Test server works without API key authentication."""
    url = f"{test_server_no_auth}/run"

    payload = {"input": "No auth needed"}

    response = requests.post(url, json=payload, timeout=10)

    assert response.status_code == 200
    data = response.json()
    assert "Echo: No auth needed" in data["output"]


@pytest.mark.e2e
def test_stream_endpoint_success(test_server: str) -> None:
    """Test /stream endpoint returns SSE events."""
    url = f"{test_server}/stream"

    payload = {"input": "Stream test"}
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {TEST_API_KEY}",
        "Accept": "text/event-stream",
    }

    response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers, stream=True, timeout=10)

    assert response.status_code == 200

    events = []
    for line in response.iter_lines():
        if line:
            decoded = line.decode("utf-8")
            if decoded.startswith("event:"):
                events.append(decoded)
            elif decoded.startswith("data:"):
                events.append(decoded)

    # Should have at least start and done events
    assert len(events) >= 2


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_deploy_config_defaults() -> None:
    """Test DeployConfig has sensible defaults."""
    config = DeployConfig()

    assert config.host == "0.0.0.0"
    assert config.port == 8000
    assert config.api_key is None
    assert config.cors_origins == ["*"]
    assert config.enable_metrics is True
    assert config.enable_docs is True


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_deploy_config_custom() -> None:
    """Test DeployConfig with custom values."""
    config = DeployConfig(
        host="localhost",
        port=9000,
        api_key="custom-key",
        cors_origins=["https://example.com"],
        enable_metrics=False,
        enable_docs=False,
        title="Custom API",
    )

    assert config.host == "localhost"
    assert config.port == 9000
    assert config.api_key == "custom-key"
    assert config.cors_origins == ["https://example.com"]
    assert config.enable_metrics is False
    assert config.enable_docs is False
    assert config.title == "Custom API"

# Copyright 2025 © BeeAI a Series of LF Projects, LLC
# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

"""Tests for the deployment CLI."""

import tempfile
from pathlib import Path

import pytest

from beeai_framework.deploy.cli import init_deployment, main


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_init_deployment_creates_files() -> None:
    """Test init_deployment creates all expected files."""
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
        created = init_deployment(output_dir=tmpdir, port=8080)

        assert "Dockerfile" in created
        assert "docker-compose.yml" in created
        assert "requirements.txt" in created
        assert "serve.py" in created
        assert ".env.example" in created

        for filepath in created.values():
            assert filepath.exists()


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_init_deployment_file_contents() -> None:
    """Test init_deployment creates files with correct content."""
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
        created = init_deployment(output_dir=tmpdir, port=9000)

        # Check Dockerfile
        dockerfile_content = created["Dockerfile"].read_text()
        assert "FROM python:3.11-slim" in dockerfile_content
        assert "EXPOSE 9000" in dockerfile_content
        assert "serve.py" in dockerfile_content

        # Check docker-compose.yml
        compose_content = created["docker-compose.yml"].read_text()
        assert "9000:9000" in compose_content
        assert "BEEAI_PORT=9000" in compose_content

        # Check requirements.txt
        requirements_content = created["requirements.txt"].read_text()
        assert "beeai-framework[deploy]" in requirements_content

        # Check serve.py
        serve_content = created["serve.py"].read_text()
        assert "from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent" in serve_content
        assert "serve_agent" in serve_content
        assert '"9000"' in serve_content


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_init_deployment_custom_entrypoint() -> None:
    """Test init_deployment with custom entrypoint name."""
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
        created = init_deployment(output_dir=tmpdir, entrypoint="main.py")

        assert "main.py" in created
        assert "serve.py" not in created

        dockerfile_content = created["Dockerfile"].read_text()
        assert "main.py" in dockerfile_content


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_init_deployment_skip_existing() -> None:
    """Test init_deployment skips existing files without force."""
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
        # Create initial files
        init_deployment(output_dir=tmpdir)

        # Modify a file
        dockerfile_path = Path(tmpdir) / "Dockerfile"
        dockerfile_path.write_text("MODIFIED")

        # Run again without force
        created = init_deployment(output_dir=tmpdir)

        # Should skip existing files
        assert len(created) == 0

        # Content should be unchanged
        assert dockerfile_path.read_text() == "MODIFIED"


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_init_deployment_force_overwrite() -> None:
    """Test init_deployment overwrites files with force=True."""
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
        # Create initial files
        init_deployment(output_dir=tmpdir)

        # Modify a file
        dockerfile_path = Path(tmpdir) / "Dockerfile"
        dockerfile_path.write_text("MODIFIED")

        # Run again with force
        created = init_deployment(output_dir=tmpdir, force=True)

        # Should recreate files
        assert "Dockerfile" in created

        # Content should be regenerated
        assert "MODIFIED" not in dockerfile_path.read_text()
        assert "FROM python:3.11-slim" in dockerfile_path.read_text()


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_cli_deploy_init() -> None:
    """Test CLI deploy init command."""
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
        result = main(["deploy", "init", "-o", tmpdir, "-p", "8080"])

        assert result == 0
        assert (Path(tmpdir) / "Dockerfile").exists()
        assert (Path(tmpdir) / "docker-compose.yml").exists()


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_cli_deploy_init_force() -> None:
    """Test CLI deploy init command with force flag."""
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmpdir:
        # First run
        main(["deploy", "init", "-o", tmpdir])

        # Modify
        (Path(tmpdir) / "Dockerfile").write_text("MODIFIED")

        # Second run with force
        result = main(["deploy", "init", "-o", tmpdir, "-f"])

        assert result == 0
        assert "MODIFIED" not in (Path(tmpdir) / "Dockerfile").read_text()


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_cli_no_command() -> None:
    """Test CLI with no command prints help."""
    result = main([])
    assert result == 1


@pytest.mark.unit
def test_cli_deploy_no_subcommand() -> None:
    """Test CLI deploy with no subcommand prints help."""
    result = main(["deploy"])
    assert result == 1

ValidationError as e: 209 duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000 210 self._metrics.record_request_end(False, duration_ms) 211 return JSONResponse( 212 status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST, 213 content=ErrorResponse( 214 error="Invalid request", 215 code="VALIDATION_ERROR", 216 details={"errors": e.errors()}, 217 request_id=request_id, 218 ).model_dump(), 219 ) 220 except Exception as e: 221 duration_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000 222 self._metrics.record_request_end(False, duration_ms) 223 logger.error(f"Agent execution failed: {e}") 224 return JSONResponse( 225 status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, 226 content=ErrorResponse( 227 error=str(e), 228 code="AGENT_EXECUTION_ERROR", 229 request_id=request_id, 230 ).model_dump(), 231 ) 232 233 @app.post("/stream") 234 async def stream_endpoint( 235 request: RunRequest, 236 authorization: str | None = Header(None, alias="Authorization"), 237 ) -> EventSourceResponse: 238 """Execute the agent and stream the response.""" 239 _validate_api_key(authorization) 240 self._metrics.record_request_start() 241 start_time = time.time() 242 243 async def event_generator() -> AsyncGenerator[dict[str, Any], None]: 244 try: 245 if self._semaphore is None: 246 yield { 247 "event": StreamEventType.ERROR.value, 248 "data": to_json(StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.ERROR, data="Server not async def health_endpoint() -> JSONResponse: 280 """Health check endpoint.""" 281 checks = { 282 "agent_loaded": self._agent is not None, 283 "server_ready": self._ready, 284 } 285 all_healthy = all(checks.values()) 286 287 return JSONResponse( 288 status_code=status.HTTP_200_OK if all_healthy else status.HTTP_503_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE, 289 content=HealthResponse( 290 alias="Authorization"), 301 ) -> JSONResponse: 302 """Metrics endpoint.""" 303 _validate_api_key(authorization) 304 return JSONResponse(content=self._metrics.get_metrics().model_dump()) 305 306 return app 307 308 async def _get_memory(self, session_id: str | None) -> BaseMemory: 309 """Get or create memory for the session.""" 310 if session_id is None: 311 memory = await self._agent.memory.clone() 312 memory.reset() 313 return memory 314 315 if not await self._memory_manager.contains(session_id): 316 memory = await self._agent.memory.clone() 317 memory.reset() 318 await self._memory_manager.set(session_id, memory) 319 320 return await self._memory_manager.get(session_id) 321 322 def _prepare_messages(self, request: RunRequest) -> list[UserMessage | AssistantMessage | SystemMessage]: 323 """Convert request input to messages.""" 324 if isinstance(request.input, str): 325 return [UserMessage(content=request.input)] 326 327 messages: list[UserMessage | AssistantMessage | SystemMessage] = [] 328 for msg in request.input: 329 if msg.role == MessageRole.USER: 330 messages.append(UserMessage(content=msg.content)) 331 elif msg.role == MessageRole.ASSISTANT: 332 messages.append(AssistantMessage(content=msg.content)) 333 elif msg.role == MessageRole.SYSTEM: 334 messages.append(SystemMessage(content=msg.content)) 335 return messages 336 337 async def _run_agent(self, request: RunRequest) -> RunResponse: 338 """Execute the agent and return the response.""" 339 messages = self._prepare_messages(request) 340 341 run_kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {} 342 if request.context: 343 run_kwargs["context"] = request.context 344 if request.max_iterations is not None: 345 run_kwargs["max_iterations"] = request.max_iterations 346 347 original_memory = self._agent.memory 348 try: 349 self._agent.memory = await self._get_memory(request.session_id) 350 result = await self._agent.run(messages, **run_kwargs) 351 352 usage = None 353 if hasattr(result, "usage") and result.usage: 354 usage = { 355 "prompt_tokens": result.usage.prompt_tokens, 356 "completion_tokens": result.usage.completion_tokens, 357 "total_tokens": result.usage.total_tokens, 358 } 359 360 response_messages = [ 361 MessageContent( 362 role=MessageRole.ASSISTANT if hasattr(msg, "role") and msg.role == "assistant" else MessageRole.USER, 363 content=msg.text, 364 ) 365 for msg in result.output 366 ] 367 368 return RunResponse( 369 output=result.last_message.text, 370 messages=response_messages, 371 session_id=request.session_id, 372 usage=usage, 373 metadata={ 374 "iterations": len(result.iterations) if hasattr(result, "iterations") else None, 375 }, 376 ) 377 except Exception as e: 378 raise AgentExecutionError(str(e), cause=e) 379 finally: 380 self._agent.memory = original_memory 381 382 async def _stream_agent(self, request: RunRequest) -> AsyncGenerator[StreamEvent, None]: 383 """Execute the agent and stream events.""" 384 messages = self._prepare_messages(request) 385 386 run_kwargs: dict[str, Any] = {} 387 if request.context: 388 run_kwargs["context"] = request.context 389 if request.max_iterations is not None: 390 run_kwargs["max_iterations"] = request.max_iterations 391 392 original_memory = self._agent.memory 393 try: 394 self._agent.memory = await self._get_memory(request.session_id) 395 run = self._agent.run(messages, **run_kwargs) 396 397 async for data, meta in run: 398 event = self._convert_event(data, meta) 399 if event: 400 yield event 401 402 result = await run 403 yield StreamEvent( 404 type=StreamEventType.DONE, 405 data={ 406 "output": result.last_message.text, 407 "session_id": request.session_id, 408 }, 409 ) 410 411 except Exception as e: 412 yield StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.ERROR, data=str(e)) 413 raise 414 finally: 415 self._agent.memory = original_memory 416 417 def _convert_event(self, data: Any, meta: EventMeta) -> StreamEvent | None: 418 """Convert agent event to stream event.""" 419 if meta.name == "update" and hasattr(data, "update"): 420 update = data.update 421 if hasattr(update, "key"): 422 if update.key == "thought": 423 return StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.THINKING, data=str(update.value)) 424 elif update.key == "tool_name": 425 return StreamEvent( 426 type=StreamEventType.TOOL_CALL, 427 data={"name": str(update.value)}, 428 ) 429 elif update.key == "tool_output": 430 return StreamEvent( 431 type=StreamEventType.TOOL_RESULT, 432 data={"output": str(update.value)}, 433 ) 434 elif update.key == "final_answer": 435 return StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.TOKEN, data=str(update.value)) 436 elif meta.name == "partial_update" and hasattr(data, "update"): 437 update = data.update 438 if hasattr(update, "key") and update.key == "final_answer": 439 return StreamEvent(type=StreamEventType.TOKEN, data=str(update.value)) 440 441 return None 442 443 def serve(self, **uvicorn_kwargs: Any) -> None: 444 """Start the server (blocking).""" 445 try: 446 import uvicorn 447 except ModuleNotFoundError as e: 448 raise ServerStartError( 449 "uvicorn not found. Run 'pip install \"beeai-framework[deploy]\"' to install.", 450 cause=e, 451 ) 452 453 kwargs: dict[str, Any] = { 454 "host": self._config.host, 455 "port": self._config.port, 456 } 457 kwargs.update(uvicorn_kwargs) 458 459 uvicorn.run(self.app, **kwargs) 460 461 462 def serve_agent( 463 agent: AnyAgent, 464 config: ModelLike[DeployConfig] | None = None, 465 memory_manager: MemoryManager | None = None, 466 **uvicorn_kwargs: Any, 467 ) -> None: 468 """Serve an agent as a production-ready API. 469 470 Args: 471 agent: The BeeAI agent to serve. 472 config: Server configuration. 473 memory_manager: Optional memory manager for stateful sessions. 474 **uvicorn_kwargs: Additional arguments passed to uvicorn. 475 476 Example: 477 >>> from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent 478 >>> from beeai_framework.deploy import serve_agent, DeployConfig 479 >>> 480 >>> agent = ReActAgent(llm=chat_model, tools=[], memory=memory) 481 >>> serve_agent(agent, config=DeployConfig(port=8080)) 482 """ 483 server = AgentAPIServer(agent, config=config, memory_manager=memory_manager) 484 server.serve(**uvicorn_kwargs) 485

Here's a summary of what was created: ## Summary ### New Module: `beeai_framework/deploy/` 1. **`__init__.py`** - Module exports for public API 2. **`api.py`** - `AgentAPIServer` class and `serve_agent()` function with endpoints: - `POST /run` - Execute the agent synchronously - `POST /stream` - Stream agent execution via SSE - `GET /health` - Health check endpoint - `GET /metrics` - Server metrics (optional, protected) 3. **`config.py`** - `DeployConfig` with settings for host, port, API key, CORS, etc. 4. **`types.py`** - Request/response types: `RunRequest`, `RunResponse`, `StreamEvent`, `HealthResponse`, `MetricsResponse` 5. **`errors.py`** - Deployment-specific errors: `DeploymentError`, `ServerStartError`, `AgentExecutionError` 6. **`cli.py`** - CLI with `beeai deploy init` command that generates Dockerfile, docker-compose.yml, requirements.txt, and entrypoint script ### Modified Files 1. **`agents/base.py`** - Added `serve()` and `create_server()` methods to `BaseAgent` 2. **`pyproject.toml`** - Added: - `sse-starlette` dependency - `deploy` extra: `["fastapi", "uvicorn", "starlette", "sse-starlette"]` - CLI entry point: `beeai = "beeai_framework.deploy.cli:main"` ### Tests: `tests/deploy/` 1. **`test_api.py`** - E2E tests for API endpoints and unit tests for config 2. **`test_cli.py`** - Unit tests for CLI and deployment file generation ### Usage Examples ```python # Simple: one-liner deployment from beeai_framework.agents.react import ReActAgent agent = ReActAgent(llm=llm, tools=[], memory=memory) agent.serve() # Starts server on 0.0.0.0:8000 # With configuration from beeai_framework.deploy import DeployConfig agent.serve(config=DeployConfig(port=8080, api_key="secret")) # Standalone function from beeai_framework.deploy import serve_agent serve_agent(agent, config=DeployConfig(port=8080)) # For integration with existing apps server = agent.create_server() app = server.app # FastAPI app for mounting ``` ```bash # CLI usage beeai deploy init # Generate deployment files beeai deploy init -p 9000 # Custom port beeai deploy init -f # Overwrite existing files ```
